Current Affairs Commentary

Prospective and Retrospective Views on the Bandit Troubles in Northern Sichuan - Ting

Examining the rampant banditry in Northern Sichuan, it originated in October of the previous year. At that time, the bandit Xu Xiangqian took advantage of the war among the Sichuan provincial armies against Liu (Wenhui) to flee from Shaanxi into Sichuan, sweeping through Tongjiang, Nanjiang, and Bazhong. He directly descended upon Suining and Yilong, establishing the "Sichuan-Shaanxi Soviet Government" in Changchi, Nanjiang, proclaiming the title of the "Fourth Front Army of the Workers' and Peasants' Red Army." He expanded his strength, growing from over ten thousand people to one hundred fifty to sixty thousand in just a few months. This did not even include the so-called "special detachments" and "guerrilla units." His rapid development surpassed that of the three bandits He (Long), Kong (Hechong), and Wu (Huanxian). The Sichuan warlords, from the two Lius downwards, including Deng, Tian, Li, and Luo, were all brave only in their selfish infighting, allowing the Red forces to grow unchecked and become a prairie fire. It was not until Liu Wenhui was defeated and fled to Xikang that Liu Xiang and others were honored with titles such as "Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression" and "General Commander," and began to feel the pain and planned their response. However, in the bandit areas of Northern Sichuan, the people killed by the bandits already numbered over a million. The tragic sacrifice, as commentators said, was unparalleled in the three hundred years since Zhang Xianzhong. Thinking of this, one cannot help but sigh and feel endless hatred.

Liu Xiang's appointment as Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression occurred around December of last year, but the order for a general offensive was delayed until October 15. According to his plan, the bandit suppression military operations were divided into five routes. The first route, under Deng Xihou, targeted Nanjiang. The second route, under Tian Songyao, targeted Yilong. The third and fourth routes, under Li Qixiang, Luo Zezhou, and Yang Sen, targeted Yingshan. The fifth route, under Wang Lingji, targeted Suining and Yilong. The advance of the five routes should have been as interdependent as the cheek and axle of a cart, responding like fingers and arms. However, at the beginning of the campaign, cracks were already evident. Among the five routes, only the fifth route, the direct line of the Liu family, was most willing to fight. Therefore, they were able to take Suixuan in one fell swoop. The next best were the third and fourth routes, which were still able to respond tactically. However, the first and second routes seemed to be estranged, watching from the sidelines. Their motivation was nothing more than to preserve their strength for future use. Later, Deng and Tian, unable to withstand criticism from all sides, began to show some enthusiasm, successively recovering Zhaohua, Jiange, and the Yilong area. At that time, although the bandits' momentum had been slightly reduced, it was still not enough to deliver a fatal blow. Unexpectedly, Liu Xiang could not wait and took the lead in announcing the demobilization plan after the end of the bandit suppression military operations, and telegraphed the Central Government to abolish the Sichuan Provincial Government and replace it with a Rehabilitation Supervision Office as the highest authority in Sichuan. Although Liu Xiang stated that the demobilization was up to each army to decide and that he would not be demanding, the other warlords, inherently suspicious, could not help but feel that they would be discarded once they were no longer needed. The impact on the future of bandit suppression was not insignificant.

After the recovery of Suining and Yilong, the first phase of the offensive plan was barely completed. January 13 of this year was set as the date for the second full-scale general offensive. However, in terms of battle achievements, only the fifth route army's capture of the Madu Pass, the only natural barrier between Tongjiang, Bazhong, Yilong, and Suining, was somewhat commendable. Moreover, even in this battle, the main reason why our army was successful was still due to infighting within the bandit forces. The bandit Xu clearly saw that the bandit suppression army was internally fragmented and that only the fifth route army was its sole enemy. Therefore, he spared no effort to fight it with all his strength. At the critical juncture of the front-line military operations, many of the other routes still stood by and watched. Over a hundred prominent figures from Chengdu and Chongqing, including Zeng Jian and Hu Jingyi, could no longer tolerate it and telegraphed the generals, urging them to arouse their conscience. Their grief and anger overflowed in their words.

After the fifth route army marched directly towards Bazhong from Madu Pass, the second and third routes also joined forces there. However, the first route army alone faced the north, providing remote support, which was actually just a show of force. After Bazhong fell, the bandits retreated to Tongjiang. According to common sense, the bandit's arrogance might have been slightly reduced. However, because the bandit area was shrinking day by day and the defensive line was shortening, their combat power was instead concentrated. Xu and the bandits believed that the success or failure of Tongjiang was extremely important, so they did not hesitate to fight the fifth route army to the death with their backs to the city. In this battle, both sides engaged in hand-to-hand combat in the cliffs, charging back and forth, sometimes gaining, sometimes losing. The losses of the fifth route army were the most severe of all battles. Its division commander, Xu Yaoqing, sent a long telegram to Liu Xiang, stating that the bandit Xu relied on natural barriers and stubbornly resisted to the death. If no measures were taken to win over the hearts of the people and cause internal division, relying solely on force would likely make it difficult to eliminate them in the short term. After the Battle of Bazhong, the fifth route army advanced deep alone, seemingly entering the third phase of the bandit suppression military operations. However, the guest armies of each route failed to advance simultaneously, resulting in three general offensives against Wanyuan, wasting manpower and money. The results were not as good as the local militia and the "Holy Mother Corps" and other civilian armed forces. On August 17, Chiang Kai-shek sent a special telegram to Liu Xiang, instructing him to order the various armies to work hard to advance and strictly prohibit hesitation and watching from the sidelines. Otherwise, the respective commanders would be held accountable. Less than a week after this telegram was sent, on August 23, the news of the Liu army's disastrous defeat in the second battle of Wanyuan came swiftly. Liu was indignant and ashamed, and resigned. I have heard that Northern Sichuan is barren and lacks food, and the autumn harvest in the Wanyuan area usually occurs around the middle of August. With this new grain, the Red bandits have provisions and salaries. It will be even more difficult to quell the rebellion in the future.

From this, it can be seen that the setback in the current bandit suppression military operations in Northern Sichuan was actually due to the failure of the five route armies to fully coordinate, resulting in wasted military spending and little achievement. Among them, the fifth route army was the most effective in suppressing the bandits, and its contributions cannot be denied. However, because it was the direct line of Liu Xiang, it was resented by the other armies. As for the other armies' watching from the sidelines, it is indeed worthy of criticism. However, in all fairness, if Liu Xiang could have known the way to win people over and not let them develop unfounded suspicions, it might not have been so. Moreover, we still remember that when the bandit Xu occupied more than ten counties in Northern Sichuan, his momentum was very strong. The various units of Tian, Deng, Yang, and Li were not secure from morning till night. Liu Xiang was indifferent. At that time, the bandit forces could have taken advantage of this situation to defeat them one by one. However, because they were eager to connect with He Long and urgently wanted to attack eastward, they were taken advantage of by Liu's forces. Therefore, Xiang himself cannot be considered an exception to the blame for the so-called failure to cooperate. A gentleman is lenient in blaming others and strict in blaming himself. I hope Xiang will calm down and reflect on himself. Recently, the Central Government has earnestly retained Xiang in his resignation and agreed to subsidize the Sichuan Province with 10 million yuan for bandit suppression. Liu Congyun, who is criticized by all parties and called a monster, has also telegraphed his resignation and the lifting of his position as the chairman of the front-line military committee. Perhaps the bandit suppression military operations in Northern Sichuan can have a turning point after this twist. However, the key to future success or failure still lies in the sincere cooperation of the various armies. This depends on the awakening of the various armies. In addition, regarding the bandit troubles in Northern Sichuan, there are two more things that should be noted. One is to strive to facilitate transportation in Eastern Sichuan and to build the section of highway from Wanxian to Yihan as soon as possible to facilitate military transportation. The second is to rigorously implement blockade measures in the border areas of Hubei, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Sichuan to prevent the Red bandits from fleeing. As for breaking the unique defensive zone system in Sichuan, prohibiting the pre-collection of land taxes, abolishing miscellaneous taxes, and unifying the currency system, all of which are related to the long-term stability of Sichuan Province, are not limited to bandit suppression, so I will not elaborate on them.

The Censorate Requests Statistics on the Suspension of Appointment and Promotion of Officials

(Nanjing) The Censorate believes that in recent years, the government has not compiled statistics on the suspension of appointment and promotion of officials, resulting in appointments and promotions still occurring, which greatly affects the power of the Censorate and the administration of officials. It has specially consulted the Examination Yuan, ordering the Ministry of Personnel to compile statistical lists and distribute them to the central and local governments, revising them every three or six months, so that the two powers of censorship and personnel administration can assist each other and those who have been impeached will not re-enter the path of office. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 1st)

Jin Wensi Telegraphs to Congratulate the Queen of the Netherlands on Her Birthday

(Nanjing) Jin Wensi, the Minister to the Netherlands, telegraphed to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs that he had followed the proper procedures to attend and congratulate the Queen on her birthday on the 4th of May. (Special dispatch on the 1st)

The Ministry of Finance Appoints Tax Officials

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has issued an order appointing Wang Wenwei as a special committee member of the Ministry's Local Tax Consolidation Association, Liu Jinyong as the acting Director of the Chahar Stamp and Tobacco Tax Bureau, He Qiaonian as the Director of the Fuzhou Consolidated Tax Administration, and Peng Shixun as the Mining Tax Collection Commissioner of Anhui, Yuhang, and Fanchang. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 1st)

Trees Must Be Planted on Both Sides of Highways

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce, in view of the increasing development of highway construction in various provinces, and the fact that the planting of trees on both sides of the highways has not been taken seriously enough, has recently requested the provincial governments to instruct the responsible officials to plan the planting of trees on highways at the same time as constructing highways. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 1st)

Simplified Rules for the Telecommunications Conference Announced

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications' Telecommunications Conference decided to open on the 4th, and preparations are nearing completion. The Ministry of Communications announced the simplified rules for the conference on the 1st, stipulating that the attendees are limited to local bureau directors, department chiefs, business chiefs, and engineers who have telecommunications administrative and engineering responsibilities. All members have been summoned and are arriving in Beijing one after another. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 1st)

Favorable Treatment for Communist Self-Reformers

(Fuzhou) The Nanchang Headquarters ordered the Fujian Province that communist self-reformers in the recovered areas who surrender to the bandit forces should be treated favorably without exception. Retaliation, extortion, or oppression are not allowed, and violators will be severely punished. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 29th)

Major Powers Reach Consensus on the Issue of Soviet Russia Joining the League of Nations

Agree to Elect Soviet Russia as a Permanent Council Member

Increasing Hope for World Peace

(Geneva) The Associated Press learned today from reliable sources that the major powers have reached a concrete understanding on the issue of Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations. At the League of Nations General Assembly meeting this month, the major powers decided to formally invite Soviet Russia to join the League. According to diplomatic negotiations conducted by various countries last week, all member states of the League of Nations Executive Council, except Japan and Germany, have agreed to submit this draft to the General Assembly. Reports that the opinions of various countries are divided and will indefinitely delay Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations are insufficient to affect this informal coordination. The members of the Executive Council unanimously agreed on the following two points: ㈠ Welcome Soviet Russia to join the League of Nations; ㈡ Grant Soviet Russia a permanent council seat on the Executive Council. The reason is that the world is heading towards war, and Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations can make peace more hopeful. The Soviet Russian government has now submitted an informal application to prepare to join the League of Nations, on the condition of obtaining a permanent council seat on the Executive Council and appointing Soviet Russian people as important committee members. As for Poland's request to be a permanent council member of the Executive Council, nothing has been heard. The annual fee that Soviet Russia should pay is 3 million Swiss francs, exceeding only the United Kingdom. (National Telegram on the 31st)

A Glimpse of the Situation Regarding Soviet Russia Joining the League of Nations - Parisian Newspapers Consider It a Major Event

(Paris) According to political news, after Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu met with French Foreign Minister Barthou, the issue of Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations is much more optimistic. The League of Nations General Assembly will be held this month, and it is expected to obtain more than two-thirds of the majority. (National Telegram on the 1st)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Barthou plans to go to Geneva on Wednesday or Thursday to attend the Executive Council meeting. However, if British Foreign Minister Simon delays leaving London until the League of Nations General Assembly, Barthou may also postpone his trip. The rumor that Barthou will go to Rome in the autumn to meet with Mussolini has now been confirmed. They will hold talks outside the League of Nations meeting, and most of the talks will focus on the preparations for the Rome meeting. King Alexander of Yugoslavia is about to visit Paris. The French government is actively negotiating with the capital of Yugoslavia regarding the reception arrangements. Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu is currently in Paris and has met with Barthou. The topics discussed include the Austrian situation, the issue of Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations, and negotiations on the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. People in Paris say that the negotiations on Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations will definitely have good results and are quite optimistic. Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations will be decided by the League of Nations General Assembly, and only a two-thirds majority of members is required to pass. In addition, the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact is still being negotiated by the countries concerned, and it seems to require considerable time. However, Soviet Russia's accession to the League of Nations and the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact are negotiated separately, and there is no connection between them. In short, the meeting between Barthou and Titulescu was based on the spirit of friendship between the two countries, and they openly discussed the upcoming discussion to be held in Geneva on September 7. (Havas dispatch on the 31st)

Sofia The League of Nations General Assembly is about to open. The Bulgarian delegation, led by Foreign Minister Batolov, will depart for Geneva on September 3. Batolov recently issued a statement to the press, saying that Bulgaria is deeply concerned about the League of Nations and that the Bulgarian nation also expresses great faith in it, because the League of Nations has fortunately avoided many serious war dangers, and the League of Nations is striving to maintain the safety and independence of small countries. Moreover, the League of Nations has given Bulgaria valuable assistance in material terms. We will not forget this sincere treatment. In short, no matter what kind of financial, economic, social, and political issues, the League of Nations conducts objective research with the most generous spirit. (Havas dispatch on the 21st)

The Hague If the issue of Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations is submitted to the League of Nations General Assembly, what attitude will the Netherlands take? The government is considering this matter. What can be determined now is that the Netherlands will never oppose Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations. However, it is not yet known whether it will vote in favor or abstain. (Havas dispatch on the 31st)

(Paris) The Parisian newspapers published in the evening all have comments on Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations. The Times editorial stated that there are various benefits to Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations, but some people oppose it. If Soviet Russia does not join the League of Nations, what benefit is there to the international community? According to the Times, after Soviet Russia joins the League, its diplomatic methods will seek to adapt to the diplomacy of Western countries and abandon its Asian policy. Soviet Russia's accession to the League is necessary for international cooperation. Even if there are opponents, they cannot prevent Soviet Russia from joining. "Hard Line Report" believes that Soviet Russia's participation in international organizations has a major impact on the international situation, because Soviet Russia has a population of 180 million, which is an indispensable factor in maintaining the world's balance of power. We must not ignore it. In theory, Geneva cannot be without Soviet Russia. (Havas dispatch on the 31st)

(Paris) The newspapers all regard Soviet Russia joining the League of Nations as the most important issue of this League of Nations session. Although Soviet Russia's accession to the League has encountered various serious difficulties, there is no doubt that it will be passed. What is unknown is whether it can get the unanimous approval of the Executive Council, so that Soviet Russia can occupy a permanent seat in the Executive Council. The Paris Echo newspaper stated that countries that sympathize with Soviet Russia must use all their strength to unite two-thirds of the majority vote in the General Assembly, so that the Soviet Russia accession plan can be passed. The People's Daily stated that for the sake of Soviet Russia's own interests and the interests of Europe and peace, Soviet Russia must join the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch on the 1st)

Japanese Air Defense Drill

Dropping Incendiary Bombs and Deploying Smoke Screens

400,000 People Mobilized in the Light Rain

Three Major Cities Seemingly Transformed into Battlefields

(Tokyo) The air defense drill in the three cities of Tokyo, Kawasaki, and Yokohama started at 3:00 PM. 400,000 members of the air defense corps were mobilized and guarded their predetermined areas, practicing shooting, protecting against poison gas, incendiary bombs, and smoke. At night, they practiced blackouts, with lights extinguished throughout the city. 300 army officers and 6,000 police officers were stationed throughout the city to enforce martial law. (Associated Press dispatch on the 1st)

(Tokyo) The joint air defense drill of the three major cities, supervised by the Tokyo United Defense Corps, was scheduled to begin at 3:00 PM on the 1st in the light rain under the slogan "Our Imperial Capital Must Be Defended by Ourselves." A total mobilization of 400,000 people had already been in a standby posture, waiting for the signal to open fire. The exercise is scheduled to last until 2:00 PM tomorrow (the 2nd), practicing real combat day and night, and will show off its offensive and defensive strategies. This day coincided with the 11th anniversary of the Great Earthquake. Dropping incendiary bombs and deploying smoke screens, the various parts of the city would be transformed into battlefields. This situation is reminiscent of the situation at the time of the Great Earthquake. At night, blackout control will be implemented, completely without lights, making Tokyo completely disappear into the darkness. The tension of the scene will be beyond imagination. (United Press dispatch on the 1st)

(Tokyo) Today is the first day of the Tokyo air defense drill. The Supervisory Department convened representatives of the defense corps of the 35 districts at Shiba Park at 10:00 AM to hold a final discussion. The various defense corps and the special corps of the various companies and department stores, women's army, and volunteer army were all ready, waiting for the enemy planes to attack. At noon, a wireless radio warned that the enemy planes were approaching, and the citizens were suddenly tense, preparing for the worst. At 1:00 PM, Tokyo Mayor Niizuka issued a warning on the radio, saying that the crisis in the imperial capital was becoming more urgent, and the people of the country must unite to protect the national territory. Then, the members of the various defense corps deployed everything in the rain, and the exercise did not begin until 3:00 PM. Because of the rain, the planes could not fly. However, the frequent warnings of enemy planes made the citizens tense. At night, the enemy planes attacked the imperial capital, so the anti-aircraft guns in various places and the exercise areas were quick to deal with poison gas and fire. The citizens participated enthusiastically and were extremely active. (Electric Electric dispatch on the 1st)

Japan Attaches Unusual Importance to the Overturned Train Case on the China Eastern Railway

Suspects Soviet Russia of Planned Action

The Truth of the Incident is Awaiting Thorough Investigation

(Tokyo) The telegram of the Yi army attacking the train on the southern line of the China Eastern Railway, killing and injuring many people, arrived at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs had considered the many facts that the train had been turned over at the time when the negotiations for the transfer of the China Eastern Railway were stalled, and paid attention to the relationship with Russia. The incident was analyzed from the following perspectives: ㈠ The accidents that have occurred in the past have only occurred on the eastern line, intending for military trains. This time, it occurred on a passenger train, and although its nature is different, the plan is meticulous and organized; ㈠ The target of the attack is specifically aimed at Japanese and "Manchurian" people, while Russians are often unharmed. The current emphasis is on the relationship with Russia. As a result, Ambassador Hishikari was asked to thoroughly investigate, and after the cause is determined, it was decided to transfer it to diplomatic negotiations, and effective measures will be taken for future security guarantees. (Electric Communication dispatch on the 1st)

Inspection of the Scene of the Incident (Harbin) The train robbery incident that occurred on the 30th on the southern section of the Eastern Railway was a rare tragedy in recent years. Especially since this case broke out in the safest southern section, and most of the victims were Japanese, it aroused unusual attention. Japanese reporters went to the scene of the incident to conduct on-site inspections, and took the ambulance that departed from Harbin at 10:30 AM on the 31st to rush to the scene. It was found that the location was ten kilometers south of Wujiatun Station, and there were small mountains on both sides of the railway, which was considered the most suitable place for hijacking a train. The joints of the railway tracks were all removed, and several trenches were dug at a distance of about half a kilometer from the railway. It can be seen that today's train robbery incident was a planned action. Moreover, there were suspicious Russian people on the ill-fated train. At the time of the tragedy, they had already fled without a trace. According to the passengers, at the time of the incident, screams of killing and slaughter were heard inside and outside the train, and Russian accents were heard in the Yi army. Combining the above situation, this case has to be regarded as a major one. (Japanese United Press dispatch on the 1st)

Suspicious Behavior of Russian Train Attendants (Harbin) The southern line of the China Eastern Railway, which was always considered absolutely safe, suddenly experienced an unprecedented tragedy, which had a great impact on the South Manchurian transportation. According to the talk of the victims, the Soviet attendants in the first and second class cars turned the light switches on and off from time to time that night, seemingly indicating some kind of signal. When the train was traveling between Wujia and Shuangchengbao, there was a loud noise. At that time, it was thought to be a derailment, but hundreds of Yi army members immediately started shooting, and the army instantly turned into a battlefield. The guards rose up to fight back, exchanging miserable gunfire in the rain and darkness. The purpose of the Yi army was to kidnap Japanese and loot property. Then they shouted and jumped into the first and second class cars, taking all the passengers of the first class car away. Sato Takeo, a professor of medicine at Seoul Imperial University and a doctor of medicine, closed the door and turned off the lights, and fortunately escaped the disaster. Six Japanese and one American were kidnapped, and they were whipped naked. Most of the dead died from trying to break free or being trampled to death. In addition to the Japanese, there were three Manchus and two Russians injured. They only asked the Russian and "Manchurian" people for money and did not harm them. (Electric Communication dispatch on the 1st)

Number of Dead, Injured, and Kidnapped (Changchun) The following is the official report received today on the victims of the accident on the southern line of the Eastern Railway: 7 Japanese and 5 Manchus died, and 22 were seriously and slightly injured. 6 Japanese, 1 American, and 1 Dane were kidnapped. (Electric Communication dispatch on the 1st)

(Harbin) The total number of people who died on the spot and died from serious injuries in this train overturning has reached ten. In addition, in addition to Uchida and Fujisawa, officials of the Resources Bureau, there are also two or three Koreans who were kidnapped. It is now found that the names of those who were kidnapped at that time are listed on the left: Hirata Kanjiro, a water transport officer of the Railway Bureau; Kawabata Tokuji, an official of the Dalian Wharf Office; Murakami Kita, an official of the Harbin Office of the Ministry of Civil Affairs; Mr. Takarazuka, an official of the Mito Company; a Danish tourist, Johnson; Matsumoto Keizo, an official of the Mito Company; and Rulli, a Japanese-American businessman who stayed in Japan's Showa Building in Marunouchi. It is said that those who were kidnapped this time were people who ran away from the sleeper car when the Yi army robbed the train. Passengers who stayed locked in the car were spared. (Japanese United Press dispatch on the 1st)

Japanese and Puppet Troops Dispatched to Pursue (Harbin) This morning, the Yamamoto Cavalry Unit of the Wakayama Unit stationed in Harbin, about 600 people, led by Captain Yamamoto, went to Shuangcheng County. There were also Japanese independent guard troops and puppet infantry troops accompanying them. It is reported that they want to thoroughly attack the Yi army and try to rescue the kidnapped Japanese. (Associated Press dispatch on the 1st)

(Harbin) Regarding the whereabouts of Engineer Fujisawa Takeo of the Japanese Cabinet Resources Bureau and five other Japanese, as well as Johnson, the manager of MGM Pictures, and Rulli, the owner of the Rulli Foreign Company in the Showa Building in Tokyo, who were kidnapped when the Yi army attacked the train on the southern line of the China Eastern Railway, the Wakayama Unit and the Civilian Affairs Department in Harbin started operations at dawn today. It was learned at 2:00 PM today that those who were kidnapped were escorted north to the Zhize area in the middle of the Songhua River in the Xujiawo tribe west of Wujia Station. Therefore, a large-scale operation has begun. Moreover, the Yi army is afraid of the pursuit of the Japanese army and dare not cross the Songhua River. Therefore, the Japanese army is now severely guarding that area and plans to wipe out the Yi army in one fell swoop. (Electric Communication dispatch on the 1st)

Night Trains Between Harbin and Changchun Suspended (Harbin) The China Eastern Railway authorities decided to suspend the night trains that depart from Harbin and Changchun at 9:00 PM, due to the threat of the Wujia Station incident. (Associated Press dispatch on the 1st)

Another Train Attacked East of Ashi River

(Harbin) The China Eastern Railway train was attacked by "bandits" again today, but they did not use the old trick of dismantling the tracks. This time, a train heading west was stopped by a fog signal 18 miles east of the Ashi River. After the train stopped, the "bandits" opened fire, injuring a Russian driver and a Chinese fireman. Although the driver was injured, he continued to drive the train east to Ertiantangzi (transliteration) and safely arrived there. As for Johnsen and Lulli, two employees of the American MGM film company who were kidnapped from the train 26 miles south of Harbin yesterday, their whereabouts are still unknown. (Reuters dispatch on the 1st)

Russian Warships Return Polish Visit

(Moscow) The flagship "Marat" and two minelayers (the "Kalinin" and "Volodarsky") of the Soviet Baltic Fleet, under the command of Commander Galerev, left Kronstadt this morning for the Polish naval port of Gdynia in return for the Polish Navy's visit to the Soviet Union last month. (TASS dispatch, 1st)

Japanese Propaganda Claims Secret German-Polish Pact; Russian Newspaper Exposes Its Intentions

(Moscow) The Tokyo Asahi Shimbun's London correspondent reported that "a secret pact exists between Germany and Poland stipulating that if Japan and the Soviet Union initiate hostilities, Germany and Poland will jointly attack the Soviet Union." The Izvestia newspaper commented on this, saying, "This prestigious Japanese newspaper, the Asahi Shimbun, is undertaking a task not usually performed by Japanese newspapers, namely, revealing secrets of war preparations. We only need to observe recent news from Japan superficially to understand that these newspapers have received orders from 'certain parties' to daily inform Japanese readers that Japan and 'Manchukuo' have absolutely no aggressive ambitions and are determined not to prepare to attack the Soviet Union. However, they claim that the Soviet Union is trying to attack Japan and Manchukuo, and that if such a conflict breaks out, Japan's military mission will be very simple because Japan will not be isolated and will receive joint military assistance from Britain, Germany, and Poland, or all three of them. However, they do not let their own readers know that the adventurist policies pursued by Japanese aggressors in the past have never caused Japan to encounter such thorough moral isolation in world public opinion as it does today. At the same time, this sensational news from the Asahi Shimbun is also noteworthy in another aspect. In order to make Japanese public opinion believe that there is indeed a secret pact between Germany and Poland regarding the Japan-Soviet war, it also uses the opposition of the German and Polish press to the Eastern Pact among other evidence. This point is particularly noteworthy." (TASS dispatch, 31st)

Direct Paris-Moscow Telephone Line Opens

Franco-Russian Relations Growing Closer

Foreign Ministers Exchange Encouraging Words

(Paris) The direct telephone line between Paris and Moscow officially opened this afternoon. First, Minister of Posts and Telegraphs Mallarmé spoke with Soviet People's Commissar of Posts and Telegraphs Rykov. Mallarmé said, "I am extremely happy to conduct a telephone call on the direct telephone line between Paris and Moscow today. Transportation and communication between the two countries will advance from this point on. This is a very good omen for the future of friendship between the two countries. I firmly believe that not only will Franco-Russian relations grow closer as a result, but world peace will also benefit." Rykov replied, "Both France and Russia are striving to maintain peace. I am certain that after the realization of telephone communication, the two countries will become closer in economic and intellectual aspects. On behalf of my country, I extend my respects to you and ask you to convey the respects of the postal and telegraph workers of our country to the workers of your country." Then, Foreign Minister Barthou spoke with Soviet Deputy People's Commissar of Foreign Affairs Krestinsky. Barthou said, "The voice of the French Foreign Minister is reaching Moscow directly from Paris via telephone line for the first time. I sincerely wish that these first few words will clearly state the close and friendly relations between France and Russia and France's full commitment to maintaining peace. The responsibility of maintaining peace is extremely important, and it can only be achieved if countries that share this goal cooperate faithfully, resolutely, and continuously. We are very pleased that Soviet Russia is willing to cooperate with France. I deeply hope that this telephone communication will greatly benefit the development of Franco-Russian friendship in all aspects." Afterward, Barthou exchanged conversations with French Ambassador to Russia Alphand, Soviet Chargé d'Affaires to France Hershfeld, and Krestinsky. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

French Newspaper Discusses the International Situation

(Paris) Le Petit Journal, under the headline "Are We About to See War Again?", studies the possibility of world peace and war. It recently published an article by reporter Berthelot, which stated, "The greatest events in human history are brewing. Ambitions, desires, and the need for survival have reached a climax. Firstly, regarding Britain, the competition between Japan and Russia is sufficient to damage its prestige and its commercial power in the Far East. If a conflict occurs between Japan and Russia, Britain will not suffer any losses. Britain's only policy is to maintain its superior power. The Netherlands is threatened by the economic bankruptcy and the trend of native revolutions. Germany is seeking advancement in the Pacific, and Poland's importance in Asian commerce is beyond what is generally expected. Next is Soviet Russia, which is watched by generally weak and small ethnic groups. That country has formed close relations with the ethnic groups of Central Asia and is also close to Japan. Japan's modern culture and industry are excessively inflated and urgently need to expand outwards. It would be difficult to confine it to the islands. Next, there is the United States. Western civilization in Asia often relies on that country as its protector. Americans want to 'whiten Asia,' thus inviting resistance from Japan, which says, 'Asia belongs to Asians.' Finally, there is China, which has been seeking unification for five thousand years and has aroused the covetousness of foreigners, so that the Pacific problem is no different from the China problem. France controls a part of Southeast Asia through Annam. France's integrity is praised by people, and it has a great mission in the Pacific, but we French people must broaden our horizons and not see the Alps as the national border." (Havas dispatch, 1st)

Chinese Military Transportation Delegation Arrives in Hamburg

Hamburg, Germany The Chinese Military Transportation Delegation, led by Vice Minister of Communications Yu Feipeng and General Xu Tingyao, arrived in Hamburg this morning. They were welcomed by the chairman of the local Far East Association and other people. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Korea Cracks Down on the Entry of Chinese Laborers

Seoul (1st) The Korean Governor-General's Office, in order to adjust the labor situation in Korea and protect the lives of laborers, decided to prohibit the entry of Chinese laborers from September 1st. The regulations are recorded as follows: (1) Those who do not carry a deposit of more than 100 yen will not be allowed to enter the country; (2) Those who do not have definite jobs will not be allowed to enter the country. The Governor-General's Office issued the following opinions on the above situation: Regulations for cracking down on the entry of Chinese laborers have long been established, but the entry of Chinese laborers has never had any impact on the Korean labor market, so it was casually overlooked. However, recently, the number has increased by 3,000 people per year, and the total is estimated to reach more than 40,000 people. Judging from this situation, if their entry into the country is allowed to continue unchecked, it will inevitably oppress the Korean labor market. Therefore, the existing rules will still be applied to crack down on the entry of Chinese laborers. (Rengo dispatch, 1st)

The King of Italy Will Make a Foreign Tour

(Paris) Le Petit Journal published a dispatch from Rome stating that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has no intention of visiting several government authorities abroad in return, but the King of Italy will soon make a foreign tour. It is now rumored in Italian official circles that the King of Italy and the President of France will visit each other, and the King of Italy will also visit London, Brussels, and Vienna in return. (Kuo Min Telegraph, 1st)

German Triumvirate Rule

(Berlin) A plan to divide the German regime and make Göring, Blomberg, and Hess a triumvirate is underway. It will be officially announced at the Nazi Party Congress in Nuremberg next week. It is learned that General Göring has now found staff to prepare for the position of Deputy Prime Minister. General Blomberg will in fact be the Deputy Commander-in-Chief of the Army, but the police maintaining domestic security will still be under the command of General Göring. Hess will still represent Führer Hitler in presiding over the Nazi Party. (Kuo Min Telegraph, 31st)

Hitler Reduces the Sturmabteilung

From 200,000 Men to 60,000 Men

A Concrete Expression of Peaceful Intentions

(Berlin) Führer Hitler's Sturmabteilung is today carrying out a reduction. The original number of members was 200,000, but now there are less than 60,000 men. The reduction will continue in the future, making it powerless to advise on politics and military affairs. This move is a complete victory for the cabinet faction, which had previously requested the reduction, citing financial reasons first, political reasons next, and finally expressing a peaceful intention towards the tense European situation. In addition, the Röhm faction argued that if the dismissed Brownshirts were not incorporated into the National Defense Force, they would oppose the dismissal, but this point was ultimately not realized. It is said that the important reason for the reduction is the excessive cost, and the right-wingers are deeply afraid that the radical faction of the Sturmabteilung has considerable power, which may be difficult to control and may cause another incident. Some aspects recognize this reduction as concrete evidence of Hitler's usual advocacy of peaceful intentions. (Kuo Min Telegraph, 31st)

The German Church Dispute

(Berlin) German Archbishop Müller, because the theological professors of Marburg in the province of Hesse-Nassau held a tough attitude towards the church dispute, wielded an iron fist today and listed Professor Hermelink in the list of retirees. He also moved the two courses of comparative religious history and religious philosophy of Marburg University to the University of Greifswald in the province of Pomerania. Therefore, Marburg is no longer a base of orthodox Protestantism. Marburg University will lose its value in the religious life of Germany. According to the university, which was built in 1527, the study of theology is well-known. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Jews Leave Germany in Succession; More Than 60,000 Have Left

(Berlin) Today's newspapers reported that after the National Socialist Party implemented the anti-Jewish movement, the number of Jews who left Germany was as follows: 21,000 to France, 10,000 to Palestine, 8,000 to Poland, 4,000 to Czechoslovakia, 3,000 each to the United States, the Netherlands, Switzerland, and Scandinavian countries, 2,000 each to the United Kingdom and Belgium, and about 6,000 to other countries. The Remarks of the President of the German Bank Cause Repercussions in France

Openly Repudiating Debts Will Close the Doors of Trade

The Market Price of German Public Bonds Plummets

(Paris) The President of the German Reichsbank, Dr. Schacht, said in a speech at the International Agricultural and Scientific Conference on the 30th that all countries should now allow Germany to simultaneously suspend payment of all debts for several years, and reduce Germany's burden to a level that it can bear when the suspension period expires. Then, the major obstacles to the revival of world commerce can be eliminated, and Germany can reappear in the world market as a legitimate buyer. French political circles now say that if payments, including commercial debts, are suspended, then Dr. Schacht will block all sources of credit and close the doors to foreign trade. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

(London) After the speech of the President of the German Central Bank, Dr. Schacht, the market conditions of various German public bonds had a violent reaction, that is, the 7% Dawes Loan of 1924 fell by 3.5 points to 47.5, and the 5.5% Young Loan of 1930 fell by 2.5 points to 36.5. According to Swiss news obtained here, the prices of German public bonds have also fallen sharply in the Zurich Stock Exchange. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

(Paris) Newspapers continue to comment on the speech made by the President of the German Central Bank, Dr. Schacht, the day before yesterday. Le Jour said, "Germany will no longer repay any debts because Germany's policy of repudiating debts has not changed from beginning to end." Le Figaro said, "Germany fears that Europe and the world will be at peace, because global chaos will give the German authorities an excuse to deal with domestic public opinion." (Havas dispatch, 1st)

International Shipping Competition

Britain Suggests Convening an International Conference

To Discuss Reducing Subsidies and Lowering Tonnage

The US Government Will Respond After Investigation

(Washington) According to Undersecretary of State Phillips, British Foreign Secretary Simon has proposed to the United States to convene an international conference to discuss reducing merchant shipping subsidies and lowering merchant shipping tonnage in order to avoid competition. Regarding this matter, the United States will first conduct an investigation and then respond to Britain. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

(London) Reuters has now learned that the British Chamber of Shipping is currently preparing to hold a conference to deal with the problem of surplus tonnage. This conference may be held in London this autumn and take the form of a special meeting of the International Shipping Conference. The British Chamber of Shipping is currently contacting similar organizations in other countries in order to implement this plan. The British government submitted a memorandum to the governments of various shipping countries on August 16, stating its views on restricting shipping. However, a meeting between governments has not been discussed at present. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

(Washington) Government officials today studied British Foreign Secretary Simon's proposed international conference to reduce shipping subsidies. The State Department has forwarded the matter to a special committee for review. There is no official expression on the US response to Britain. Within the government, opinions are divided on continuing shipping subsidies. France, Germany, Italy, Spain, and Portugal are the main European countries that insist on subsidizing shipping, but the attitudes of Britain and the United States are relatively moderate. However, the competition that the two countries are currently facing makes it necessary for them to change their shipping policies. President Roosevelt recently declared that the United States intends to develop shipping and is determined not to transfer US shipping rights to foreign countries. Therefore, if the countries fail to conclude an agreement before the end of this year, a shipping war will inevitably occur. British Minister of Commerce Runciman declared that he intends to apply to Congress for £2 million in the autumn to support British ships for one year. (Kuo Min Telegraph, 31st)

The United States Will Issue New Bonds

Silver Coin Circulation Exceeds 100 Million Yuan

Accounting for 20% of All Currency

(Washington) The US government does not want to use gold profits to redeem the maturing public bonds. According to the Treasury Department's news today, the government will issue new bonds to pay for the $124.6 million in 4.5% Liberty Bonds that are due on October 15th. As for the terms of the new bonds, they will be announced later. The $52.5 million in treasury bonds that are due on September 15th will also be handled in this way. (Reuters dispatch, 1st)

(Washington) The United States has more silver bonds in circulation today than ever before. The Treasury Department announced today that the silver coins and silver bonds in circulation are worth US$749,254,839, which represents a profit of US$107,459,249 from the government's implementation of the New Deal. The circulation of silver coins is increasing by 10 million yuan per week. The forms of this currency vary, either in silver or in banknotes. Unofficial estimates estimate that the silver coins in circulation will soon reach 100 million yuan, which is about 20% of the total currency in the United States. (Kuo Min Telegraph, 31st)

General Strike Order Issued in the US Cotton Textile Industry

(Washington) The Cotton Textile Workers Strike Committee has issued a general strike order, and the wool industry workers have also decided to join. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

(New York) There is no hope of averting the textile workers' strike in the United States. Tomorrow, 425,000 workers will stop working, including the woolen industry. According to Strike Committee Chairman Gorman, although the notice of the woolen industry strike has not yet been issued, it will definitely follow the same steps as the cotton textile workers. The woolen industry workers decided to act in concert with the cotton workers because the woolen industry rules authorities refused to convene a meeting of representatives from both sides. Strike leaders estimate that another 150,000 people will also join the strike. The textile workers in the southern states are preparing to fight to the end, and their leaders are confident that they will be able to force employers to accept their demands for increased wages, limited working hours, non-discrimination against union members, and the right for workers to assemble and negotiate. It is estimated that 150,000 cotton workers in the New England states will strike. The Boston police have discovered that the local Communist Party has received instructions to patrol the strike. The police are closely monitoring the activities of certain people. However, there is still a glimmer of hope in the strike atmosphere in the South, that is, tens of thousands of members of so-called company unions have agreed not to join the strike. The National Labor Relations Board is still working hard to achieve a peaceful resolution as soon as possible and is considering organizing an impartial committee to investigate their dispute impartially. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

The Great Fire in the Argentine Oil Depot Has Not Been Extinguished

(London) The fire in the oil depot in Campana City has lasted for several days, and other oil storage tanks have also exploded and spread. After Malaya Restricted the Import of Cotton Textiles

Japanese Goods Suffer a Severe Blow

Singapore Special Dispatch Since the British Malayan government promulgated the law restricting the import of cotton textiles, the import of cotton textiles from various countries has been greatly affected. Because Japan has implemented a dumping policy in recent years, it has suffered an even more severe blow. According to the report of the local government's Statistics Bureau, from the beginning of this year to May 7, when the law restricting the import of cotton textiles was promulgated, the import of cotton cloth to Malaya totaled 57 million yards. The annual import volume in the previous year was about 100 million yards. Calculated in the past few months, the import of Japanese cotton textiles has exceeded the legally permitted import volume of 6.5 million yards according to the restriction law. The detailed rules of the restriction law stipulate that the excess import volume before the promulgation of the restriction law this year can be deducted from the import volume next year. Now, the excess amount in this country in the past few months has reached the aforementioned 6.5 million yards. The amount of import permission that Japan should have obtained next spring will be equivalent to blocking its import in addition to this deduction. However, this only applies to white cotton cloth. As for dyed textiles and rayon, there is still a little room for maneuvering. In short, Malaya's restriction on the import of cotton textiles has indeed dealt a fatal blow to the import of Japanese cloth. Japanese cotton textile importers here have already fallen into a very miserable situation.

International Commercial Telegraph

September 1st Reuters Exclusive Market Report

(Gold and Silver) London Gold Price Today's gold price rose again, reaching 141 shillings and 5 pence, an increase of half a pence from yesterday.

London Silver Bullion In the London silver market, China and speculators sold in large quantities today, causing both spot and futures prices to fall by .1875. The spot price is 21.6875 pence, and the futures price is 21.75 pence. Indian purchases stabilized the market.

The opening price for British-American exchange was $4.99125, which was .125 lower than yesterday's closing price for American-British exchange. At 11:00 AM, it rose .25 to $4.99375, but it closed down .625 to $4.9875.

British-French This morning's opening price was 74 francs 56, an increase of three pounds from yesterday's closing price. At 11:00 AM, it rose another three pounds to 74 francs 59, but the closing price fell by six pounds to 74 francs 53.

American-British In the New York foreign exchange market, the pound fell .625 this morning, and the American-British exchange rate was $4.98625. The market was extremely quiet. At 10:40 AM, this price remained unchanged.

(Cotton and Wheat) Liverpool Wheat The closing price for October Liverpool wheat was 5 shillings 9.625 pence, down .25.

Liverpool Cotton The Liverpool cotton market closed today, down one pound from yesterday. The price for October was 6.88.

New York Wheat The New York wheat market opened with some contract prices unchanged and others down .125. The market was extremely calm before noon. At 10:40 AM, the May contract was down .25.

New York Grains Grain opened with prices down .125 to .25. It continued to fall before noon, mainly due to a large number of deliveries. At 10:40 AM, the market price fell again by .25 to .375.

(Securities) New York Factors favorable to the market before the opening of the securities market were: (1) Although the securities market situation was uncertain, no significant pressure was found when prices fell; (2) Steel industry work will increase by 10% to 16% starting on the 1st of next week, which is the starting point of the autumn turnaround. Factors unfavorable to the market situation were that the textile industry strike has spread to the woolen industry. When the securities market opened this morning, the market situation was very sluggish, and various securities fell slightly. Mining stocks fell by one pound under slight pressure, such as US Steel. The market is calm as the holidays approach, and there seems to be no important trend for the time being. The securities market prices are listed on the left.

Conflict of Authority Between Two Japanese Agencies Stationed in the Puppet State

Caused by Smuggling Cases

The Situation Has Become Serious

According to the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun of August 23rd, at a time when the reform of institutions in Manchuria is being advocated seriously, the sudden conflict of authority between the two major agencies, the Kwantung Government and the Embassy, is a major ominous phenomenon in national politics. After "Manchukuo" took over the Dalian Customs last summer, it raised the tax rate. Therefore, smuggling cases in the Kwantung Leased Territory on the border between Manchuria and Korea have been occurring frequently. The amount of smuggling of cotton cloth, rayon, sugar, woolen fabrics, etc. has gradually increased, and the authorities' crackdown has already become a major issue. Unexpectedly, on July 12th and 13th, a large-scale organized smuggling incident was discovered in a Manchuria Railway freight car between Pulandian and Wafangdian in the Kwantung Leased Territory. The principal offender was a worker in the Wafangdian Manchuria Railway engine district. The offender was arrested by the Wafangdian Kwantung Leased Territory Police Station, which led to the expansion of the case. The Yingkou Military Police Detachment believed that the prosecution by the Wafangdian Police Station was slow and that there were suspicions of malfeasance by a number of police station officers. Starting on August 4th, they conducted a thorough investigation in the Tianjia area of Wafangdian for four days, involving more than 100 people. More than 20 police officers were suspected and escorted to the Yingkou Military Police Team, and then transferred to the consulate. The Yingkou Consul, seeing the abnormality of the incident, in order to avoid the advisor to the Kwantung Government Police Department, telegraphed the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to assign the responsibility of interrogation in order to thoroughly investigate whether the police officers had committed any illegal acts. This matter is currently under investigation in Yingkou, and the Kwantung Government authorities believe that the actions of the Yingkou Consul are not only illegal, but also deliberately trampling on the dignity of the Kwantung Government and tarnishing the prestige of the Kwantung Government Police Officers. They are greatly dissatisfied with this act of exceeding authority. On the one hand, it is believed that the conspiracy of this case has a major relationship with Councilor Tani Masayuki. The future changes in the situation deserve close attention.

The Eastern River in Guangdong Floods, Downstream Disaster Areas Suffer

Refugees in Shangdong, Dongguan, Urgently Awaiting Relief

Over 500 Houses Collapsed in Pingshan District, Huiyang

Guangzhou Correspondence, The big flood in the lower reaches of the East River in Guangdong Province has caused disaster. A breach of more than 200 zhang occurred in Shangdong Village, Dongguan County. The water depth in and out of Huiyang City is more than one zhang, as high as the eaves. The situation of the disaster has been briefly recorded in previous reports. Now, although the flooding is gradually receding, after the heavy flooding, the people in the area are almost destitute. The damage to the destroyed roads cannot be counted. There are about 1,500 refugees in Shangdong Village, Dongguan, still living on the hills, waiting to be fed. The village had a breach once 20 years ago. In recent years, the river management committee loaned funds to repair it, and the funds have not yet been repaid. Now it has suffered this tragic calamity again, and it will not be able to restore its vitality after a hundred years. Yesterday, representatives of the refugees from the village went to the province to appeal to the authorities for relief to save the remaining lives of the thousands of disaster victims. As for Huiyang, the water level was highest on the 24th of this month, with a water depth of more than 1 zhang and 2 chi on flat ground. Fortunately, the weather cleared up and the flooding receded quickly. Traffic has gradually resumed. According to a post-disaster investigation, the Pingshan area of the county is located in the upper reaches of the West River. Mountain floods arrived suddenly and were not easy to discharge. Pingshan Market became a flooded area. More than 100 residents were drowned because they could not escape. 18 houses collapsed in the market, 21 in North Gate Street, 9 in the Lumberyard, 17 in Caotang Street, 12 in Shakangwei, 18 in West Gate, and 23 in Mahuang Temple. In various villages, the number of collapsed houses is: 37 in Qiaotian Township, 21 in Longguizhang, 33 in Hetou, 27 in Waliao, 24 in Duchaotou, 30 in Qinglongtan, 22 in Wenbu, 27 in Buxinwei, 26 in Xiaopu, 34 in Lingzitou, 25 in Dazhou, 26 in Qinghe, and 37 in Huangzhuli. A total of 503 houses collapsed. The roads are full of starved corpses, and the situation is especially tragic. Also, hundreds of houses collapsed in the Baimanghua area. More than 100 people were trapped in the water and fortunately rescued. All crops were lost, and the fields have become wilderness. In the Sanduozhu area, the loss of materials and engineering for the Pingrong Highway exceeded 10,000. One bridge was destroyed in the Pingduo section, and the roadbed was leveled for more than 80 chi. In the Duoxin section, a large bridge 110 chi long was washed away by the water. The water depth on the flat ground was more than 1 zhang, and traffic was cut off. It was an unprecedented disaster in the area. At the moment, mourning cries are everywhere. The county party headquarters and various groups have sent telegrams to the provincial government requesting that funds be allocated quickly for disaster relief to ensure the safety of the people. (August 28th)

Northeastern Population Survey

Changchun Has Become a World of Japanese and Koreans

Changchun Correspondence, There have never been accurate statistics on the population of the Northeast. The following is a compilation of the number of households in the Northeast surveyed by the Puppet State Council last year, as well as the population surveys of Japanese, Koreans, and foreigners in Changchun, Harbin, and Qiqihar this year.

Northeastern Population At the end of last year, the total number of households in the Northeast was 5,186,000, and the population was 30,088,000. Compared with the previous year, the number of households increased by 356,000, and the population increased by 1,274,000. By gender, there were 17,001,000 men and 13,879,000 women, a ratio of 122 women per 100 men. By nationality, there were 30,019,100 Chinese, 591,000 Japanese, and 98,000 other foreigners. As for the number of households in the Kwantung Leased Territory and the South Manchuria Railway Zone, there were 337,000 households and a population of 1,409,000, an increase of 23,000 households and 85,000 people compared to the previous year. By gender, there were 832,000 men and 577,000 women. By nationality, there were 1,098,000 Chinese, 309,000 Japanese, and 2,000 other foreigners. Adding the previous figures, the total is 5,423,000 households and a population of 32,288,000, an increase of 369,000 households and 1,358,000 people compared to the end of the previous year. The total population of Japanese living in various parts of the Northeast and the Kwantung Leased Territory reaches 900,000, an increase of 6 people compared to the end of the previous year, excluding Koreans.

Changchun Survey Since the puppet took the stage, the Japanese and Korean population in Changchun City has increased greatly, and it has become a world of Japanese and Koreans. As of the end of July this year, the number of Japanese has increased to more than 3,000. The statistics are as follows: (1) 108 Japanese households, 2,325 men, and 1,562 women; (2) 417 Korean households, 1,325 men, and 933 women; (3) 85,657 Han Chinese households, 323,651 men, and 270,010 women; (4) 1,961 Northeastern "Banner People" households, 3,964 men, and 2,829 women; (5) 154 Mongolian households, 260 men, and 190 women; (6) 801 Hui Chinese households, 2,570 men, and 1,729 women.

Harbin Japanese Residents Before the Incident, there were only over 1,000 Japanese residents in Harbin. After the Incident, the number increased sharply. According to a survey by the Japanese Consulate Police Department, in June of this year, there were a total of 3,274 Japanese households in Harbin, with a population of 11,248, a decrease of 62 people compared to May. Brothels and opium dens account for the majority of the residents.

Foreign Residents in Jiang Province According to a survey by the Qiqihar Puppet Police Department, the household registration of foreigners residing in Heilongjiang Province in July of this year is as follows: (1) 86 White Russian households, 218 men, and 174 women; (2) 3 Red Russian households, 3 men, and 1 woman; (3) 2 American households, 1 man, and 4 women; (4) 4 German households, 4 men, and 2 women; (5) 2 Swiss households, 2 men, and 3 women; (6) 3 Polish households, 4 men, and 3 women; (7) 2 Norwegian households, 2 men, and 4 women. A total of 102 households, 234 men, and 191 women.
