Reports by Kong Hechong at the Memorial Week Ceremony of the Acting Headquarters

Kong Hechong, the former commander of the Red Bandit's pseudo-Sixth Army Corps, surrendered and attended the Memorial Week ceremony of the Acting Headquarters last month on the 20th. He reported on the overall collapse of the Red Bandits, the gist of which was recorded in this newspaper on the 24th. Now, we further supplement the full text of Kong's report as follows:

"Chairman and Comrades, it is a great honor for Hechong to participate in the Memorial Week of the Premier today. However, upon self-reflection, I feel only shame and apprehension. I am ashamed of having strayed onto the wrong path and made grave mistakes. I am apprehensive because I am but a humble person under your command. Yet, I am grateful to Chairman Chiang for not blaming my past and treating me with exceptional courtesy. This magnanimity makes me feel deeply indebted and without a place to hide myself. As for my background, I am especially grateful for the Chairman's introduction just now. Now that I have the honor of attending this grand meeting, I can only report my past experiences in three parts as follows, as a reference for eliminating bandits and as a contribution to express my gratitude: A. My aspirations for surrendering; B. The actual situation in the bandit areas; C. Personal opinions.

Now, let me first talk about Part A. Since I joined the pseudo-Soviet revolution in 1927, eight years have passed. My original intention for participating was to fight for the interests of the masses, not for personal gain. However, after eight years of trial, the result was the opposite of my original intention. Not only did the political level decline day by day, but the lives of the masses also became more and more painful. They were completely deceived by the Communist Party. This is clear proof that communism is not viable. Therefore, a new feeling arose. Since 1927, I have held considerable positions in the Soviet government, from commander to commander-in-chief. However, after examining the country, society, and people's livelihood, I finally realized that it was a kind of blind obedience, and what I saw was an inhuman life. Because China is not an industrialized country, there is no such thing as a bourgeois or proletariat. The masses are all poor. There is fundamentally nothing to share, but they insist on using a strong hand to carry out the so-called common ownership. Therefore, the result is only getting worse and worse. This is the reason why communism cannot be realized. Furthermore, regarding their strategy, initially they were made to follow the Qiu Bai line by the Third International, which was deemed an opportunistic line. As a result, it was considered rash action. Following this was the Li Lisan line, which soon failed and was unworkable. Then there was the Luo Ming line, the Bolshevik line, and various other lines. Not only did they still fail, but they also caused those who claimed to be leaders to have factional differences and endless internal strife. From this, it is even more evident that China absolutely cannot implement communism. This is an undeniable fact. Only the Kuomintang's Three Principles of the People conform to China's national conditions, the modern environment, and can be realized to save China. Therefore, I resolutely made the greatest determination to surrender and return, not for fear of hardship, nor for promotion and wealth, but entirely to seek to save the suffering masses, eliminate the Red Bandits, and realize the Three Principles of the People under the leadership of Chairman Chiang. This is the general meaning and aspiration of my coming here.

Next, I will talk about the second part, the actual situation in the bandit areas. Since the Communist Party implemented the land revolution, they have supposedly adopted the land distribution policy of the Marx and Lenin era. However, at one time, they advocated confiscating the land of landlords with more than 100 mu, and at another time, they advocated confiscating all land and redistributing it. As a result, the masses did not gain any benefit but were first subjected to the levies and corvée labor, which was simply deceiving the suffering masses as tools for the bandits to seize power. Recently, they have also said that the masses are willing to go to the front lines as Red Army soldiers to call on the masses to be sacrificed. In fact, no one is willing to go; they are all forced to go. At the moment, there are no able-bodied men in the bandit areas, and complaints are rampant, which is the reason. Secondly, the pseudo-commander-in-chief has now changed his strategy in military matters. First, he uses the pseudo-First, Third, and Fifth Army Corps as the main force to resist the National Army in the main areas, and uses the pseudo-Seventh and Ninth Army Corps to contain the National Army in the secondary areas. Second, he organizes various guerrilla teams in an attempt to disrupt the rear of the National Army. Third, he assembles the main force, attacks the weak points of the National Army, and seeks opportunities for battle, implementing short and rapid assaults. Fourth, he strengthens the power of the masses. This is the recent strategy of the bandits. Another combat tactic is that each squad is equipped with a skilled marksman to individually shoot at the targets of the National Army. But evil cannot defeat good, which is natural. All kinds of cunning schemes have been defeated by the National Army. As a result, they are only waiting to die. Furthermore, since the National Army implemented the blockade, rice, salt, and so on have been almost cut off. The bandit guerrilla teams cannot move freely. The banknotes issued by the pseudo-central government, which were more than ten million when I left, are not in cash. It costs one yuan to buy one tael of oil and salt. The source of income depends entirely on various taxes. The budget for taxes in the bandit areas can only support three or four months. There are still eight or nine months of expenses, which completely depend on looting the local tyrants. Now that the local tyrants have been looted, the masses are forced to do the so-called "saving campaign." They have already saved more than three sheng of rice twice, eight sheng of rice twice, and five sheng of rice twice. Even vegetables must be saved by the masses to supply them. This kind of coercive measure is partly due to the tight blockade, which prevents oil, salt, and food from entering the bandit areas, and at the same time, the products of the bandit areas cannot be sold. Especially since the fifth encirclement and suppression, the bandit areas have gradually shrunk. The general masses are very dissatisfied with the pseudo-Soviet Communist Party and want to join the National Army. This is a glimpse of the psychology of the masses in the bandit areas. Furthermore, the main force of the bandits cannot overcome the fortress policy. In particular, the soldiers are most afraid of airplanes and cannons. Especially in every war, they are defeated, and their lives are extremely painful. Therefore, the number of people coming to surrender is gradually increasing. This is proof of the strength of the bandit army. Now there are 200,000 people recruited in the rear, including men and women, all of whom are forced to come. Every batch sent to the front line runs away. Now the effective forces are the pseudo-First, Third, Fifth, Seventh, and Ninth Army Corps, a total of twelve divisions and five teaching divisions. Each regiment also has independent battalions, special service companies, guerrilla teams, and so on. The rest of the bandit army is either understaffed or has insufficient firearms and no training, making them vulnerable. The above is all the actual situation in the bandit areas.

Now, let me talk about the third part, my personal opinions on the bandit areas. How to eliminate bandits and how to prevent bandits from ever occurring again? We should refer to the above-mentioned actual situation in the bandit areas to attack the weaknesses of the bandits. In my opinion, the most important thing is to start from the political aspect. First, the issue of organization. The organizational strength of the masses in our country is weak. We should step up the organization of the masses. With the masses, we can use their strength to transform everything. For example, the bandit army totals only more than 100,000 people. Why do we need so many National Army soldiers to fight them? This is because the Red Army uses numbing methods to grasp the masses and use them for their purposes. Second, the issue of training. Once we have the masses and the organization, we still need to strengthen training and education. At present, culture is backward, and the knowledge of the masses is immature. The Communist Party uses this weakness to loot the local tyrants and numb the masses. And the masses, being ignorant, are actually deceived by them. Therefore, we must strictly implement special education. The method should be to use the Three Principles of the People to overcome the Communist Party's deceptive tricks of the land revolution. Only in this way can we make the people believe in the Three Principles of the People, and bandits will never occur in China again. Third, winning over the masses. The issue of the masses is paid attention to by all countries in the world. Even Germany, after its defeat, revived by grasping the masses. At present, there are about 2 million people in the bandit areas. Their talents, military force, economy, transportation, etc. are all inferior to ours. And everything we have exceeds theirs. If we can grasp these 2 million people in our hands, the bandits will be eliminated by themselves. Because bandits completely rely on the masses for survival. If we try to win over the masses, it will definitely be very easy. However, there are a few things to pay attention to. First, our declarations or leaflets should not write the words "bandit area masses." Because the word "bandit" makes the masses afraid to look at them. They don't look at them at all. Second, the text should be simple and easy to understand, so that the masses can easily understand it. And it should not only be in vernacular Chinese, but also include a few more notes to give them a good impression. This is the way to win over the masses. The above are all political aspects. Secondly, in the military aspect, the most important thing now is to attack the weaknesses of the bandits. First, bandits are most afraid of airplanes and cannons. We should prepare more airplanes, bombs, and cannons, and pay special attention to the bandits' fortifications. Second, we must strengthen the blockade line. The blockade is very loose in areas such as Ganzhou Yuanjiangkou. Food enters and exits every day. We should especially strengthen the blockade and not relax it at all. Third, pay attention to the longitudinal and transverse bunkers. We should immediately strengthen the bunker policy and build more longitudinal and transverse bunkers, so that the bandits have no chance to escape in the terrain area. As I speculate, the Communist Party will probably flee to Guizhou and Sichuan in the future. Because Guizhou and Sichuan have dangerous mountains, inconvenient transportation, can live independently, and have backward cultures. The masses are easily anesthetized. If we don't pay attention, it will be difficult to eliminate them. Therefore, strengthening the blockade and the bunker policy, so that not a single bandit can escape, is the most important thing. In short, I have come this time with the greatest determination. In the past, I worked 14 or 16 hours a day. Now I am willing to work a few more hours. My will is that if the bandits are not eliminated in one day, I will not let go in one day. Now, under the leadership of Chairman Chiang, the soldiers should unify their will and resolutely eliminate the bandits and revive China. This is my personal aspiration."

Hubei Provincial Government Implements Joint Office

All Departments and Offices Vigorously Streamline Personnel and Reduce Government

Monthly Savings of 30,000 Yuan

Hankou Correspondence: The joint office of all departments and offices of the Hubei Provincial Government, after a long period of preparation, will be implemented on September 1st. The implementation measures have been approved by Chairman Chiang. In general, all official documents will be collected and distributed by the Provincial Government and decided on in the name of the Chairman. Subordinate agencies directly under the departments and offices may issue orders directly. Submissions to the Provincial Government will be changed to signed reports. Communication between departments and offices will still be done by official letters. All accumulated cases were completely handled on the 31st. Reorganization was implemented, and the list of staff was also announced on that day. It is found that the Provincial Government originally had three sections, which have now been reduced to two. Four offices have been added: technical, legal, statistical, and public bulletin. Monthly expenses have been reduced from more than 23,000 yuan to more than 17,000 yuan. The Department of Civil Affairs originally had three sections, with the addition of a land section and a opium prohibition office. Now there are still three sections, and the opium prohibition office has also been changed to a section. The first, second, and third subsections of the first section have been merged into one subsection, and the fourth subsection has been abolished. The first subsection of the second section has been merged with the second subsection of the first section. The original expenses of more than 22,600 yuan have been reduced to more than 17,000 yuan. The Department of Finance originally had four sections, which have now been reduced to three. The original expenditure of more than 22,000 yuan has been reduced to more than 16,000 yuan. The Department of Construction originally had four sections, which have been reduced to three. Monthly expenses have been reduced from more than 13,000 yuan to more than 9,900 yuan. However, the Department of Education still has three sections, and the reduction of personnel is also relatively small. In total, the departments have laid off about 100 people, and expenses have been reduced by more than 30,000 yuan. The Security Office originally had staff, adjutants and other offices, with sections under the offices. Now they are all merged and changed to the Director's Office, with three sections under it. Because the candidates for the director and deputy director have not been determined, the reorganization will take some time. As for the criteria for this layoff, inspectors, general affairs and accounting staff are all laid off. Section chiefs, subsection chiefs, and section staff are laid off at discretion. Those with service experience are still transferred to other agencies for appointment, or given external positions at discretion. (August 31)

Songjiang

Tragic News of Suicide Amidst Unemployment

Yang Guangzu, residing at No. 4 Hualiang Temple Lane in this county, is over sixty years old. He used to be a foreign coppersmith in Singapore. His wife, Chen, is about the same age. They have a son and three daughters. Their son, Yunpeng, works at Xie Da Xiang silk shop in Shanghai. The eldest daughter is married to the Shi Mei Ting family, and their family is happy. Recently, it was learned that the factory in Singapore closed down, and he was quite worried about unemployment. He was unhappy at home. Suddenly, this morning at about five o'clock, he secretly used a razor to commit suicide by stabbing his throat. Fortunately, the neighbors discovered it and called his son-in-law to send him to Songjiang Hospital for treatment. His life is not in danger. This is also tragic news amidst the recession.

Taicang

Septuagenarian Forcibly Assaults Young Girl

Wang Mao'er, a resident of Yong'an Township, Pengjian Town, belonging to this county, is a drummer. He is seventy years old but still lustful as ever. On the night of the 29th of last month, Wang suddenly had a brutal nature. He sneaked into the home of his neighbor Hu Shengfu and, taking advantage of the fact that no one was around, scared Hu's ten-year-old daughter, A'er, and silenced her. He forcibly defiled her. After the girl cried and told her father, Wang Mao'er was handed over to the watch post of the Public Security Bureau of the town that night for custody. The next day, he was sent to the main bureau with a document and transferred to the county. Shen Cheng, the examiner, opened an investigation court and ordered the coroner to examine the body in court. The court ordered the victim to be sent to the hospital for examination. The defendant, Wang Mao'er, was sent to the county prison to be held pending verification.

Near the No. 101 iron bridge on the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway in Suzhou, when the night train arrived there on the 31st, suddenly a passenger jumped off the train while the vehicle was moving slowly and tried to escape. Wuxi

County Administrative Meeting Opens

The third county administrative meeting of this county officially opened yesterday (1st). The preparations for the early stage have been recorded in this newspaper. Yesterday morning at nine o'clock, the opening ceremony was held in the county government. The attendees were Yan Shenyu, Ye Dezhen, Yu Tanfen, Qian Sunqing, Gui Wochen, Qian Zhongliang, and other 30 people. The chairman was County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, and Qian Sunqing was elected as the vice chairman. After the formalities were completed, the chairman first stated the opinions of the meeting, saying that since the second county administrative meeting in this county, after the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the social economy has been extremely panicked. Up to now, looking ahead and looking back, there are many difficulties for the administrative economy of this county, and we urgently need to find ways to provide relief. However, the bad habits of previous meetings were often that many things were discussed but not decided, and decisions were not implemented. It is hoped that this conference should, within the possible scope of human and financial resources, try its best to implement the proposals and find ways to alleviate the current difficulties, and so on. After the chairman finished his statement, guests and members Gui Wochen, Qian Sunqing, Hua Yizhi, Gao Jiansi, and Xue Mingjian successively delivered speeches. Then, the members of the proposal review committees of each group were nominated, and Qian Sunqing was designated to convene the finance group, Gao Jiansi was designated to convene the education group, Chen Zhanru was designated to convene the autonomy group, Cheng Jingtang was designated to convene the public security group, Rong Desheng was designated to convene the construction group, Hu Pinfang was designated to convene the agriculture and forestry group, and Gui Wochen was designated to convene other groups. At this time, it was already noon, so the meeting was adjourned for lunch. In the afternoon, the members of the review committees of each group separately convened review meetings to review the proposals of each group. This morning, the proposals of the finance group and the public security group will be officially discussed. This afternoon, the proposals of the education group and the construction group will be discussed.

Registration of Opium Addicts Begins

The Opium Prohibition Committee of this county held its third meeting at the county government at 2 pm yesterday and decided that registration of opium addicts, due to the urgency of the deadline, should begin on September 1. The registration and licensing methods are as follows: in the urban area, register with the county government; in each township, the registration shall be handled nearby by the district offices and the public security bureaus. As for the opium cessation permits, they are divided into two types, A and B, according to regulations. The first fee for a Type A permit is six yuan, and the first fee for a Type B permit is six jiao. Both are replaced once a year, and the permit fee is doubled each time. At the same time, the Civil Hospital was designated as the acting opium cessation center.

Disputes over the Opening of the National Goods Market

The Wuxi National Goods Exhibition, organized by the Shanghai China National Goods Promotion Society, came to Wuxi to set up a market to sell goods at the original site of the National Goods Market. It was originally scheduled to open on September 1. Before the event, more than ten trade associations, such as silk, cloth, foreign goods, cotton textiles, etc., in Wuxi, in view of the fact that previous national goods exhibitions in Wuxi had caused repeated disputes at the end, and even used low-quality goods to impersonate national goods to deceive customers, were still afraid of repeating the previous mistakes, so they went to the Chamber of Commerce to question them. The Chamber of Commerce did not have anyone to contact them beforehand, and also because similar national goods markets in Nantong and Yangzhou had caused great disputes. According to the letter from the county to inquire and also advocate that the exhibition principle should not be violated, and it should not be exclusively set up as a business, during this time of market depression, it is not appropriate to speculate on dumping and absorb domestic cash. The county government approved the letter and immediately notified the business that it should not set up a market to sell goods before negotiating properly with the various industries. Therefore, the market is now only exhibiting to all sectors and not doing business. On the one hand, the representatives Shen Mengshi and Gu Jianchen, the executive director of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, explained to all parties.

Zhenjiang

Zhenjiang-Yangzhou Long-Distance Telephone Completed

The Jiangsu Construction Department's long-distance telephone project for the twelve counties north of the Yangtze River has completed the laying of lines between Yangzhou, Taixian, Taixing, Jingjiang, Nantong, Rugao, Dongtai, Yancheng, and Funing since it started construction. Those who requested calls were very enthusiastic. Recently, the laying of underwater lines between Zhenjiang and Yangzhou has been completed. Starting yesterday, the counties south of the Yangtze River and the above-mentioned nine counties north of the Yangtze River can directly communicate, and the sound transmission is very clear. It is also heard that the Construction Department, in order to promote the use of long-distance telephones by the public, welcomes all sectors to try it out. From now until the end of September, it is specifically designated as the trial call period. The tolls for the line segment north of the Yangtze River are only charged at one-quarter of the rate. Furthermore, the three counties of Ganyu, Guanyun, and Donghai will also be able to communicate in mid-September. The underwater line between Jiangyin and Jingjiang has also been assigned to an engineer to rush to lay it.

Su People's Office Examines Water Police Chiefs

Director Yu of the Su People's Office, in view of the necessity of assessing the chiefs of the various water police districts and teams, ordered all districts to comply, since many have not yet been commissioned, and ordered them to come to the province for the examination immediately. It is now learned that Liu Wenzhou, the inspector of the fourth district and fifteenth brigade, Li Zhen, the inspector of the first branch team Jingkou Xun, and Xu Wenquan, the inspector of the second branch team Bajiangkou, were transferred to the office for the examination yesterday. The second examination was in health subjects, such as class training. After separate examinations, they were still ordered to go to their original posts and await instructions.

Sangu Canal Water Level Continues to Rise

The water level of the Sangu Canal in Zhaoguan Dam, Jiangdu Xun, was one zhang, three chi, three cun, and four fen on the 18th of this month. As of the 30th, it has risen to one zhang and four chi. According to the river workers, if there is no decrease in the increase, the Jin Pass Dam will be opened to draw water into the Yangtze River, so as to divert it appropriately.

The Wind of Robbery is Rampant in the Four Townships

Since the eight summers, there has been a long drought and no rain, and the autumn harvest is hopeless. People are panicked. Therefore, robbery cases have occurred frequently recently, and people cannot sleep peacefully. In front of the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall in the county and city a daytime robbery case actually occurred, which is truly shocking. Bandits Active in the Eastern Township

Bandits are actively operating in the various districts of the eastern township of Tongyi. The Nantong District Security Command has specially transferred a security team to suppress them. Young Arch-Thief Re-Tried and Exempted from Death

The arch-thief Qin Jinchang rampaged in the Siyu area, robbing and killing people. He was captured by the police and militia and sentenced to death by the court. Later, the High Court sent him back for a retrial on the grounds that the bandit was not yet sixteen years old. The criminal court has now changed the sentence to life imprisonment.

Lianshui

The Militia Team Suffers a Crushing Defeat in Suppressing Bandits

Zhu Zongwen, the district chief of the second district of this county, selected young militiamen from this district and the Liangcha Town area to form a militia team of more than 50 people to suppress bandits when encountering bandit police, because the Guzhai was lost and the loss was unhelpful. On the afternoon of the 26th, Zhu heard that the Huai'an-Lianshui two-county guard teams were suppressing bandits in Sunjiazhuang, so he went to help suppress them. When the officers and soldiers arrived, the bandits fled. As a result, 19 militiamen were killed and two were injured. Four male and female hostages were intercepted.

Hungry People in the Four Townships Rob Rice

The Hantang area south of this county is inherently barren, and this year's drought has exhausted the farmers' food supply. Local ruffians such as Wang Xiaodi incited poor farmers to rob rice in nearby townships. For a time, more than 100 people gathered, blew bamboo tubes as a signal, and robbed from house to house. The robbed families, feeling sorry for the hunger of the people, did not report to the officials to investigate. In addition, in the Qianbang, Gejiawan, and Pengjiawei areas south of Dayun Temple, dozens of hungry people form groups every day, holding tools and breaking into people's homes, robbing rice when they see it. The township chief flew to report to the Zhongdai Town Guard Group and sent a team to suppress it. The hungry people dispersed when they heard the news.

Yulin Bus Accident on the Mountain

The Yulin Road Company bus, carrying passengers at 5 pm on the 31st, suddenly encountered a bus of the Yuhang Public Security Bureau police while passing the mountain road of Xiaobaiyang Mountain in Yuhang. The bus, which was carrying more than 20 policemen, suddenly fell from the mountain into the fields more than three zhang below. Fortunately, the cylinder did not explode, but all the policemen were injured. Chen Ziyun and Wang Bing were the most seriously injured and were hired to be sent to the Hangzhou Municipal Hospital for treatment.

Ningbo

Farmers in Cixi Plead for Famine Relief

Farmers in the various townships of Cixi have been gathering in the city for days to petition the county government for famine relief. On the morning of yesterday (30th) at 11 am, more than 1,000 farmers from Xiangao and Mingshan townships, and Ye Ruichang and other farmer representatives from Jinchuan township, entered the city in a big way to petition the county government. Qian Zushou, the chief of the first section of the county government, received them. The farmers demanded four points: (1) There is money in the countryside but nowhere to buy rice. Please order the rice merchants to quickly identify the rice to help. The county government replied that it would order the public security bureau to urge the rice merchants to handle it quickly. (2) Submit to the provincial government to allocate money for disaster relief. The answer has been forwarded. (3) Survey the disaster and exempt the rent. The answer is that it should be handled accordingly. (4) It is forbidden to pre-rent farmland. It is forbidden by law. However, if the rent has been collected last year, should it be claimed back from the owner if the crops have not been harvested this year? Wait for the provincial government to instruct. The farmers were satisfied and dispersed.

Bandits Resist Arrest and Shoot Farmers

In the Hujia area of Qianyandang Temple, Dongyan Township, Er District, Zhenhai, there is a person named Jin Wenzhang who raises ducks for a living. The night before, he took three or five hired workers and released ducks on the Majiaqiao River in the township. He saw four people coming from the Tuanchiao side and returning to the township's Banqiao, going back and forth four times. Wenzhang became suspicious and knew they were not good people. Before long, he saw one of them wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants, wearing white ash sneakers, and holding a flashlight, wandering around nearby. Wenzhang immediately shouted that there were thieves, and took the hired workers to twist him. At that time, the local farmers Sun Anxin and Chen A'wu heard the sound and came out to see. The four people were indeed bandits. The other three saw that a thief was arrested, and they took out their pistols and shot at the farmers. A bullet hit Sun Anxin's right waist, a vital part, and he fell to the ground and died immediately. Chen A'wu was also hit in the right shoulder and escaped with his wound. The farmers also fled when they saw this. The captured bandit was still taken back and escaped along the original road. Afterwards, the responsible public security bureau reported to the Zhenhai County Government for inspection and to arrest the murderer and investigate the matter.

Local News

Yang Hucheng's Reception of the Press Yesterday

Discussing the Stability of Shaanxi and the Gradual Recovery of Rural Areas

Troop Reduction in Progress, Focusing on Afforestation and Road Construction

According to the Central News Agency, Yang Hucheng, the Pacification Commissioner of Shaanxi, has been very busy entertaining various circles since arriving in Shanghai from Xunyang on the 29th of last month. Yang Hu, the director of the Shanghai Security Office, along with Du Yuesheng, Huang Jinrong, Zhang Xiaolin, and others, hosted a banquet at the Cathay Hotel at 12:30 PM yesterday. Yang Hucheng also met with reporters from various newspapers at the Cangzhou Hotel at noon, releasing a written statement as follows:

(Purpose of Coming to Shanghai) I was summoned by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to go to Jiangxi to receive instructions and to report to Chairman Chiang on the pacification of Shaanxi and the recent situation of my headquarters. Therefore, I left Shaanxi on the 13th of this month and met with Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang and Director He Chengjun in Hanzhong. On the 17th, I arrived in Guling and met with Chairman Chiang several times, and was ordered to give a speech to the officer corps. I arrived here by plane on the 29th of last month, intending to meet with Song Ziwen, the chairman of the National Economic Council, for the second time to discuss matters related to the construction in Shaanxi by the NEC and the banking sector, as well as to treat my dental illness. After these matters are completed, I will go to Nanjing to meet with President Wang Jingwei before returning to Shaanxi.

(Stability of Shaanxi) Since 1927, Shaanxi Province has suffered from military and political turmoil, coupled with continuous droughts, leading to the proliferation of bandits and widespread poverty. Since my army was ordered to enter Shaanxi in 1930, we have believed that political clarity requires social stability. Therefore, we actively focused on suppressing bandits, and after a year, we largely eliminated them. In the past two years, due to timely rainfall, the disasters have gradually decreased. In addition, the people are eager for peace, so the bandit suppression has been even more successful. Various bandit leaders have been captured and brought to justice one after another, and the territory is very stable. As for the bandit Xu Xiangqian, who occupied northern Sichuan, he was rampant for a while, but after repeated encirclement and suppression by the Sichuan, Shaanxi, and Gansu armies in the Chengkou and Wanyuan area, I don't know what the recent situation is since I left the province 20 days ago. The defense of southern Shaanxi is firmly secured by the 38th Army of my headquarters, under the command of Sun Weiru. Although there were small-scale intrusions into the border area some time ago, they were immediately repelled by the garrison. The reports in the foreign press a month ago that Zhenba in southern Shaanxi had fallen are completely untrue.

(Troop Reduction) To permanently eliminate banditry and reduce the burden on the people, we must implement production and construction, and reduce the size of the army. Therefore, after my army cleared the various bandit gangs, we immediately followed the instructions of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to reduce the size of the troops and implement the soldier-worker system. Since receiving the order last year, we have reduced the size in stages. Since March of last year, we have reduced the size three times, cutting a total of more than 20 regiments and more than 20,000 officers and soldiers, saving approximately 4 million yuan in military expenses annually. The remaining troops have now been reduced in size and are undergoing rigorous training.

(Afforestation and Road Construction) Shaanxi Province is located on a plateau and often suffers from drought. Therefore, we first implemented soldier-worker afforestation. Due to the limited number of saplings, this spring my headquarters only planted more than 160,000 trees. We have now discussed with the provincial government and tentatively designated 200,000 mu of official wasteland on both sides of the Wei River as an area for soldier-worker afforestation, planning to plant 5 million trees. With 20,000 people planting 50 trees each per year, we can complete 5 million trees in five years. In ten years, the trees will be forested, and each tree is valued at two yuan, for a total of over 10 million yuan. We also promote the atmosphere of civilian afforestation in order to make it universal. In addition to planning to divert the Luo River to benefit the fields with a part of the military force, we are also actively building highways. There are four main lines: the Xi'an-Lanzhou, Hanzhong-Baihe, Xianyang-Yulin, and Xi'an-Hanzhong highways, totaling 1,897 kilometers. There are six branch lines, totaling 1,136 kilometers, for a total of 3,033 kilometers. Except for the stone engineering and bridge culverts, which are contracted by the NEC, all the remaining earthwork is undertaken by my headquarters. Currently, 913 kilometers of main and branch line earthwork have been completed, and the rest is still under construction. In addition, in order to practice excavation skills, we specially select one officer from each company to organize a soldier-worker road construction practice team to practice on-site with the stone and earthwork staff of the NEC to prepare for the stone engineering after the earthwork is completed. In addition, we have agreed with the provincial government to organize the Huanglong Mountain Reclamation Bureau. We have now dispatched a regiment of soldiers to first eliminate the bandits in the mountains, then station troops, and finally civilian settlements.

(Promoting the New Life Movement) Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek launched the New Life Movement, it has swept the country in a few months. The New Life Movement is a national salvation movement. In addition to issuing the New Life Movement Guidelines and New Life Movement Outlines promulgated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to all officers and soldiers, ordering them to strictly comply, we also organized a New Life Movement Inspection Team to inspect once a week to promote implementation.

(Rural Recovery) As for the social situation in Shaanxi in recent years, after years of disasters, the local vitality has been greatly depleted. However, in the past two years, the weather has been favorable, the countryside has gradually recovered, and the people's lives have gradually become stable. The central government pays attention to the construction of the Northwest and has specially set up an office of the NEC in Xi'an. Chairman Song Ziwen has worked tirelessly and even personally went to Shaanxi this spring to inspect and guide, assisting the local government in building roads and developing water conservancy. Bankers and industrialists in Shanghai have also come to Shaanxi to set up branches, preparing to invest and lend money to the countryside, which has greatly benefited the people. Especially since Chairman Shao Lizi took office, he has worked hard and achieved remarkable results. However, all production and construction must be based on social stability, and the Communist bandits must be eliminated as soon as possible. In this regard, my army, under the leadership of Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, vows to take full responsibility for suppressing them in order to lay the foundation for the construction of the Northwest.

(Bandits Will Be Eliminated) During this trip to Jiangxi, I was ordered by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to inspect the Nancheng area and meet with Commander Gu Zhutong. The Jiangxi bandits are at the end of their rope. According to my inspection, they can definitely be eliminated before the Fifth Plenary Session. In recent decades, our nation has been declining day by day. During my trip to Jiangxi, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, even in the hot summer, worked tirelessly for the public good. This spirit of perseverance and dedication to the country and the people is a model for the people of the country. The people of the country should deeply reflect on this and quickly emulate it, so that the revival of the nation can be hoped for.

(Going to Nanjing in a Week) In addition to releasing a written statement, Yang Hucheng also answered questions from reporters, saying that he came here to seek medical treatment for his dental illness. After several treatments by dentist Xu Zifeng, it has gradually recovered, but it has not fully recovered, so he still needs to stay in Shanghai for a week before going to Nanjing to visit President Wang Jingwei and then returning north. Since arriving in Shanghai the day before yesterday, he has met with Song Ziwen and others to further discuss matters related to the construction of the Northwest by the NEC and the investment of the Shanghai banking sector in the Northwest, but no final decision has been made. Shaanxi's revenue and expenditure can now be balanced.

We have yet to see or hear how the Sichuan government will comply, and the farmers, merchants, and workers are already largely displayed in a fish market. We believe that the central government, at the beginning of national construction and national revival, will not allow any provincial executive to delay or feign compliance, obstructing the progress of the major policy. Local executives are not allowed to participate in opinions or interfere and obstruct. We are extremely grateful and pray. The Chairman of the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce of the Republic of China, Lin Kanghou, kowtows with seal." All American Wheat Loans Have Been Shipped to Shanghai

322,198 Tons

A Total of 43 Sea Vessels Were Loaded to Shanghai

250,000 Tons of Flour are Also Being Loaded

Since the start of shipping our purchased American wheat on credit on November 18 of last year, the original agreement was for US$6 million to purchase 322,198 tons of wheat, to be fully shipped by the end of June this year. Another 250,000 tons of flour, worth US$4 million, must also be shipped at the same time. When the American wheat was shipped to Shanghai, the market price of flour was only 1.9 yuan per bag, which was extremely uneconomical. Therefore, the American wheat was shipped first and sold to various flour mills in Shanghai at an average price of 4 to 4.2 yuan per bag, which is equivalent to 70 yuan in national currency per ton. Among the ships used for shipping, 23 were chartered by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and 20 were chartered by the American Na-Deng-Lie-Lin, for a total of 43 ships. If the United States had not experienced a strike, all of this American wheat would have been shipped to Shanghai long ago. There are still three ships, about 27,000 tons, that have been delayed and are now arriving one after another. Yesterday, the Victoria City vessel entered the port, carrying 8,500 tons of wheat, which is the 42nd ship, currently docked at the No. 12 and 13 wharf for unloading. There is also one last ship, carrying 8,700 tons of American wheat, which, according to a telegram received yesterday, is also en route and will arrive next Saturday. When this batch arrives in Shanghai, all 322,198 tons of American wheat will be completely shipped to Shanghai. From the arrival of the first batch on November 18 of last year to the completion of the shipment, it will take a total of 9 months and 20 days. All the wheat that has been shipped has been sold out, with 95% delivered in Shanghai. The sold wheat price is approximately 22.55 million yuan in national currency. There are also 250,000 tons of flour, and we have now received confirmation that, because the market price of flour in Shanghai has soared to 2.67 yuan, the American side is purchasing it. The Cotton and Wheat Management Office is currently dispatching ships to transport it. According to the reporter's investigation, this loan of flour will be shipped to China, with some unloaded in Shanghai and the rest directly shipped to Tianjin to be sold in North China, which can avoid future transportation costs. North China's flour sales are very smooth, and domestic flour is not enough to meet demand. Therefore, this large batch of American flour will be supplied to the people. At the current market price, 250,000 tons are worth approximately 14 million yuan in national currency, which, combined with the wheat price that has already been sold, totals approximately 37 million yuan in national currency.

Down 1.2 Yuan Compared to Last Week

Shanghai Social Bureau Prohibits Exceeding the Price Limit

Shitouhezi On June 16, a bloody battle was fought with a large Japanese army at Shitouhezi in the boundary of Mishan County. After holding out for a day and a night, the Japanese army was defeated. In this battle, 30 Japanese soldiers were killed, 30 rifles, 5 trucks, 28 horse-drawn carriages, and a large amount of grain, fodder, and ammunition were seized. Our army suffered only 7 casualties.

Banjiehe On July 30, a close battle was fought with 800 Japanese soldiers guarding the barracks at Banjiehe in the boundary of Mishan County. The Post Office Starts Registering Books for Purchase Yesterday

The Date for Implementing Purchases on Behalf

Still Awaiting Determination and Announcement

The Shanghai Postal Administration issued a notice yesterday, stating: "According to the Ministry of Communications Postal Administration General Order No. 1382, forwarded by the Ministry of Communications Order, in order to promote culture, a method for post offices to purchase books on behalf is established. Attached are the Regulations for Post Offices to Purchase Books on Behalf, the Rules for Application for Registration of Post Offices to Purchase Books on Behalf, and the Compilation Format for Book Purchase Catalogues, all in one copy. Registration will begin on September 1. Anyone who meets the qualifications stipulated in the Rules for Application for Registration of Post Offices to Purchase Books on Behalf and entrusts the post office to handle it in accordance with the Regulations for Post Offices to Purchase Books on Behalf may apply to this Administration for registration in accordance with the registration rules. The registration fee is one yuan per book. However, for books published before October of this year and registered with this Administration before October 31, only a registration fee of one jiao will be charged per book to show encouragement. The registered books will be included in the catalogue by the Postal Administration General Office in accordance with the Compilation Format for Book Purchase Catalogues. In order to ensure rapid and accurate compilation, the publisher should, in the application for registration, in accordance with the classification method of books stipulated in Article 1 of the Compilation Format for Book Purchase Catalogues, indicate which of the 19 categories the book applying for registration belongs to, so that it can be catalogued by category. If it is not indicated, the post office will only rely on the book name listed on the application for registration, or may need to review the original book or send inquiries back and forth due to the inability to accurately classify it, which will inevitably cause delays. It is hoped that the publishers will pay attention. As for the handling fee for post offices to purchase books on behalf, although it has been temporarily set at 25% of the actual price for textbooks and 20% for other books, if publishers in various places are willing to negotiate better terms in order to have the post office sell their books as much as possible in various places, they must clearly state the most favorable terms in the application for registration so that the post offices in various places can be informed accordingly. Please do not wait and see and delay yourself. As for the date of implementation of purchases on behalf, it will be determined and announced separately after the catalogue is completed. All regulations can be obtained from the local post office. This is a notice from the Acting Postal Chief Zha Peilin (on official business), Acting District Deputy Postal Chief Wang Weisheng."

City Farmers' Association Sent Members Yesterday to Investigate Agricultural Disasters in Various Districts

Scheduled to conclude within a week

Proposed submission to the Municipal Government for relief

The City Farmers' Association has prepared to investigate agricultural disasters in all seventeen districts of the city. Representatives were dispatched to various districts yesterday to conduct investigations. After the investigation is completed, a meeting of representatives will be convened to discuss concrete measures and request assistance from the Municipal Government. Details of the situation are recorded as follows:

Departure yesterday morning: The city's farmland area is divided into seventeen major districts. The City Farmers' Association appointed the heads of each district and preparatory committee members to carry forms and conduct investigations by district. All departed yesterday morning, including Liu Zhaoxing in Wusong, Zhu Wenxiang in Yinhang, Xing Xin in Yinxiang, Wu Ziju in Jiangwan, Shen Wenbin in Zhabei, Hou Shizhang in Pengpu, Gu Tongchun in Pusong, Gu Junqing in Fahua, Wu Ruzhang in Caojing, Shen Ruolu in Hunan, Hu Zhu San in Yangsi, Xu Baoming in Yangjing, Cui Xing in Gaohang, Qian Hengxiang in Gaoqiao, and in Zhenru, Tangqiao, and Luhang, these three districts were assigned directly by the City Farmers' Association to staff members Jin Wenyuan, Xiao Huiqing, etc., to depart for investigation because the Farmers' Association has not yet been established. The investigation procedures are scheduled to be completed within one week.

Scope of investigation: The scope of the investigation of agricultural disasters specifies two aspects: the actual damage of the drought and the situation during the drought. Regarding the disaster situation: (1) the percentage of the disaster area in the entire district, (2) the names of the disaster sites, (3) the losses suffered by crops: (A) percentage of rice, (B) percentage of cotton, (C) percentage of beans, (D) percentage of other crops, (total number of disaster-stricken households, regarding drought prevention work: (1) the condition of water draining work, (2) the condition of farmland after water draining, (3) the condition of dam construction, (4) the total expenses used for drought prevention, (5) suggestions for drought prevention.

Nanyang Overseas Chinese Lin Aimin and Others Pioneer Overseas Markets for National Products

Organizing the Xinghua National Products General Branch to Provide Widespread Supply

Entrusting the China National Products Production and Sales Company to Solicit Samples

Among the places where our country's national products are sold abroad, the Nanyang Islands have always been the most prosperous. There are more than six million overseas Chinese who have pioneered and operated in that area. They have always worked hard to use and promote national products. However, since the rise of the European War, the Japanese have taken the opportunity to rise up and have spared no effort in pursuing Nanyang trade. Overseas Chinese in our country, due to the lack of support from the domestic production community, have found it difficult to compete alone. Therefore, up to now, the Japanese have become the number one exporter to Nanyang among all countries, while our country, which has always regarded Nanyang as its only export market, has retreated behind others and suffered a setback. Minister Chen of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, aware of this, was deeply worried and has ordered the International Trade Bureau to carefully formulate measures to seek development. Now, overseas Chinese Lin Aimin and others have initiated the organization of the Xinghua National Products Company and entrusted the China National Products Production and Sales United Company in this city to collect samples and will send personnel to Shanghai to discuss everything. The details are recorded below:

(Organizing the Company) Currently, many wealthy overseas Chinese merchants in Singapore, Nanyang, believe that the decline of our country's Nanyang trade and the Japanese squeeze are a major relationship, and that the important reason is that production and sales are lacking joint efforts. Because Nanyang does not have a specific organization to promote national products, domestic factories have many concerns and hesitate to move forward. Overseas Chinese in Nanyang also find it difficult to unify promotion steps due to the decline of national products exported to the south. With scattered individual trade, whether in main force or work, it is not enough to compete with the planned trade of the Japanese. Now, in order to promote the sales of Chinese national products and develop the Nanyang market, they have specially raised funds to establish the Xinghua National Products Company, first establishing the general company in Singapore, and planning to establish branches in various islands of Nanyang, in order to achieve widespread supply. The general company has now been organized and has entrusted the China National Products Production and Sales United Company at 261 Nanjing Road, Shanxi Road, to purchase samples on its behalf.

(Joint Production and Sales) The letter roughly stated, "There are a large number of overseas Chinese from our country, with more than six million in the Nanyang area alone. Most of them are concerned about their homeland and are happy to use national products. If there are excellent national products that meet the demand and promotion is effective, the future hope is unlimited. However, in recent years, the dumping of Japanese goods has been extremely fierce, and all our national products have been hit. In the future, overseas merchants must sincerely cooperate with domestic manufacturers to unite their strengths. It will be difficult to make progress, and I am afraid that the original sales market will decline day by day, and the rights and interests will overflow, which is painful. The colleagues have seen this, and organized the Xinghua National Products Company, which is mainly engaged in the promotion of national products. Now a general company has been established in Singapore, and in the future, it is planned to expand branches in various parts of Nanyang. The general company is now ready and will open soon. We have always admired your company as the general group of national products and hope that you will give us more preferential treatment than usual to overseas national products merchants. In order to seek various samples of goods, please inform us in detail of the prices and preferential measures, and the general agency regulations, so that we can purchase them." (Omitted below)

(Purchasing Samples) After receiving the above letter, the China National Products Production and Sales United Company, in order to promote the sales of Chinese national products and develop foreign trade, in addition to publishing a notice to all national product factories, from September 1st to October 31st, to send personnel to bring the same samples and wholesale prices, agency regulations, etc., to come to negotiate, and also sent letters to various national product factories to seek cooperation (the letter is omitted).

(Dispatching Personnel to Shanghai) After the Xinghua Company entrusted the China National Products Production and Sales Company to collect samples and solicit cooperation from various factories, for the convenience of purchasing national products, Cui Jun was specially sent to Shanghai to review various national products suitable for sale in Nanyang so that they can be transported to Singapore for layout in the short term. The China National Products Production and Sales Company has prepared everything, and it is known that since the company announced the notice, various national product factories in this city have been very enthusiastic in coming to negotiate. Also, the company moved from 500 Ningbo Road, Henan Road, to 261 Nanjing Road, Xilu Road. Later, because there were many people coming to negotiate, for the convenience of handling affairs, the old address on Henan Road is still working as usual.

Various Parties Unable to Raise Large Sums for Dredging Wusong River

Fear of another de facto standstill

Central News Agency: Regarding the dredging of the Wusong River, the central government has repeatedly convened relevant parties to discuss solutions. The Municipal Government has sent Tan Wenqing, the second section chief of the Public Works Bureau, to attend. At that time, it was decided that the city would be responsible for raising 200,000 yuan. It was originally planned that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce would raise 100,000 yuan, the Shipping Association and the Inland River Shipping Association would raise 50,000 yuan, and the Municipal Government would allocate 50,000 yuan. Therefore, the Jiangsu Provincial Government sent a letter to the Municipal Government the other day to present the fundraising situation to the central government. However, according to the news obtained by the Municipal Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce is unable to raise 100,000 yuan because it borrowed funds for dredging the Wusong River on behalf of the association in 1924, which has not yet been repaid. The Inland River Shipping Association and others, regarding raising 50,000 yuan, convened a meeting and, after discussion, also stated that they were unable to bear it. At a time when the city treasury is stretched, the Municipal Government cannot independently allocate this huge sum. Therefore, this case will come to a de facto standstill.

Seafarer Qualification Timeliness Issue Shipping Opportunity Submits for Explanation

The Seafarer Examination Committee organized by the Ministry of Communications has conducted four seafarer examinations. The Examination Committee of the Examination Yuan previously raised questions about whether it was an examination. The Ministry explained in a letter that the qualification was for on-the-job seafarers to be screened. On July 1, the Seafarer Examination Committee was automatically canceled, and the remaining certificate issuance matters were assigned to the Navigation Affairs Department for handling and changed to on-demand examinations. A marine engineer named Wang Qingfeng wanted to exchange his certificate because his service qualifications met the requirements for exemption from the exam, but the Ministry misunderstood the regulations. The United Marine Engineers Association specifically presented a rebuttal. The original text states, "It is presented because the approved reply is unclear and there are doubts. The reasons are specifically stated, hoping that you will review and follow the instructions. Regarding the application of the seafarer to exchange the Class A Marine Engineer Certificate, the China United Marine Engineers Association forwarded the Ministry's No. 2632 reply on the 10th of this month, stating that it has been received, checked, and Wang Qingfeng received the Class A Marine Engineer Certificate in December 1928, and only served on the Fuqing ship for three years and three months, and his qualifications do not meet the requirements of Article 1 of the Training Order No. 3239. The request for exemption from the exam and issuance of the certificate cannot be approved. You should immediately instruct the officer to report to the Ministry at any time for examination, as per the previous reply." After reading this reply, I was panicked and full of doubts. I will raise the points of incomprehension in order (1) Article 1 of Training Order No. 3239 clearly states that "seafarers who have obtained the captain or marine engineer certificate issued by this Ministry and have served in the positions listed on the certificate for more than five years," should be interpreted as referring to the qualifications before obtaining the certificate. If it is interpreted as after obtaining the certificate, not only is the meaning of the word "ever" not logically correct, but it is also inconsistent with the exemption method for seafarers who have not obtained a certificate in Article 2 of the same order, which states that "they have served in the position for more than ten years." Because this type of seafarer has never obtained a certificate at all, if the qualifications before obtaining the certificate are not recognized as valid, then where did the qualifications for more than ten years come from? Therefore, things are the same, and it can be understood by analogy (2) The validity period of the seafarer's certificate is five years, and the service qualifications for exemption from the exam are more than five years. If the service years before obtaining the certificate are not counted, then the five-year validity period of the certificate is insufficient, and what about the words "more than five years"? Is it not that the articles of the regulations contradict each other and cannot be self-consistent? (3) According to the original reply, the seafarer's service qualifications are valid from the date of obtaining the certificate. By analogy, I am afraid that none of the marine engineers who have obtained a certificate in the future who are subject to the original level examination will be able to pass, because the fifth item of Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations on Seafarer Examination states a total of eight years. In this method of exchanging certificates once every five years, is it not that each exchange will cancel the qualifications once, and how can the word "total" in the total of eight years be combined? Thinking quietly, can I not be speechless? Based on the three points listed above, the current regulations and the original reply have different meanings, and there must be a problem that has not been clarified, which makes people unable to adapt. For this reason, I have prepared a document to specifically state the reasons and hope that you will review and follow the instructions. It is really for the convenience of the public."

Total Import and Export of Chinese Medicine in Seven Months of This Year

Exports are mostly cinnamon, rhubarb, and licorice

Imports of American ginseng, amomum, and cardamom are still high

Zhu Dian, editor of Guanghua Medical Magazine, visited Wang Boyan, a statistics specialist at the International Trade Bureau, the other day to inquire about the recent import and export situation of Chinese medicine. According to the discussion, from January to July of this year, the export of Chinese medicine has gradually increased compared with the past. The types and quantities of exports include cinnamon 51.606 (quintals), worth 1.023.866 yuan, other cinnamon products 1.792 (quintals), worth 38.479 yuan, rhubarb 9.746 (quintals), worth 519.826 yuan, licorice 4936 (quintals), worth 346.495 yuan, Poria cocos 4.669 (quintals), worth 168.458 yuan, ginseng 149 (kilograms), worth 4.138 yuan, betel nut 67 (quintals), worth 1.044 yuan, medicines and nine powder plasters worth 141.543 yuan, imported fennel 4 (quintals), 170 (gold units, the same below), betel nut 6.429 (quintals), 78.397, amomum and cardamom 199.029 (kilograms), 173.445, American ginseng 1.921.384 (taels), 961.977. Although the export of Chinese medicine has gradually improved, there are still many imports of American ginseng, amomum, cardamom, betel nut, and other items. In view of this, Guanghua Medical Magazine plans to fully use the authority of public opinion to awaken people in the national medical community to reduce the use of foreign drugs and, when prescribing, try to replace them with other drugs within the possible range, so as to stop the leakage. At the same time, it will cooperate with the Rural Medicine Improvement Society to first start from the branch societies in Sichuan, Shaanxi, Yunnan, Guizhou, Shanxi, and Henan provinces to investigate the actual situation of Chinese medicine producing areas and improve the planting, harvesting, and preparation methods using scientific methods in order to seek overseas sales and save the declining rural economy.

Mayor Wu, considering that the number of residents in the city center is increasing daily and that it is inconvenient for them to purchase daily necessities from afar, has specially ordered the Shanghai City Xingye Trust Society to build a vegetable market in an area with dense residential population. The society, adhering to the Mayor's aim of prospering the city area and facilitating the public, has accelerated the completion of the overall plan. All the columns of the building will be made of reinforced concrete and will be equipped with toilets and modern sanitary facilities. On both sides of the vegetable market, ten city-owned houses will be added to open small-scale department stores, selling various daily necessities and Chinese and Western medicines at prices identical to those on the market. Tenders for this project will be invited soon, and it is expected to be completed within the year. It is said that the style of the vegetable market and city-owned houses will be very novel, and the rent will be extremely low, making it even more convenient for residents in the city center.

Lin Huantang Accused of Abandoning His Wife and Living with a Japanese Woman

Police Filed Public Prosecution

Lin Found Not Guilty Yesterday

Lin Yuting, a native of Taishan, Guangdong, accumulated hundreds of thousands of dollars by running a pharmacy. He recently died of illness last month, leaving behind multiple wives, concubines, and children. His son, Lin Huantang, now 28 years old, married Li Fengchun, a woman from his hometown, in Guangzhou in 1922 through a matchmaker. After marriage, the couple's relationship was initially harmonious. Later, because Lin wanted to study abroad, he left his beloved wife six months after the wedding and went overseas to study in the United States. He has been there for several years. Although he once returned to China, he soon left his wife again for the United States. This time, Lin Huantang returned after completing his studies, but unexpectedly, Lin had met a Japanese woman named Mishi in the United States and brought her back to Shanghai. As a result, the two women could not share a husband, and conflicts arose in the family, with constant quarrels. In the end, Lin favored the beautiful Japanese woman and even mistreated his wife, making her live elsewhere and neglecting to provide for her. Li Fengchun was furious and hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the First Special Court. After the trial, it was ruled that, according to law, spouses could not file lawsuits against each other, and the case was dismissed. However, Lin believed that Li's actions had severed the bond between them, so he also hired a lawyer to file for divorce in the civil court. This case is currently being heard. Unexpectedly, Li Fengchun, unable to bear the fact that her husband favored a foreign woman, living freely and treating his wife like discarded shoes with frequent mistreatment and abandonment, in addition to filing a counterclaim in the civil court and requesting litigation relief, also hired lawyer Ge Zhaoji to report to the Chengdu Road Police Station, requesting a public prosecution. This was approved, and the Special Court issued a summons yesterday morning to bring Lin Huantang to the Eighth Criminal Court, where Judge Wu Tingqi held a hearing. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, stated that he was filing a public prosecution against the defendant Lin Huantang for abandonment under Article 310 of the Criminal Law, and stated that the plaintiff Li Fengchun married the defendant in Guangzhou in 1922 and lived with him for six months before the defendant went to the United States to study in the Republic of China.

Land Price Tax Still Levied on Profitable Charity Land

The Shanghai Charity Federation sent a letter to various charities stating, "Regarding the petition submitted by this Federation to the Shanghai Municipal Government on August 30, No. 2068, requesting exemption from land price tax for charity land without profits and requesting a 50% reduction for land with profits, all have been received. The Financial and Land Bureaus have replied stating, 'We have investigated the case of the Shanghai Charity Federation's request for reduction or exemption of land price tax on the organization's land. We have previously received instructions from your government to review and discuss this matter. Our bureau, etc., have jointly reviewed and discussed the case. Regarding the part of the land with profits, although the organization has presented the difficulty of funding and submitted a budget of income and expenditure, which was forwarded by the Social Bureau for consideration of reduction or exemption, the exemption of land price tax should be limited to land that meets the requirements of Article 2, Section 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Land Price Tax Collection, which is used for public charity purposes and has no profits. Now that the land in question has profits, land price tax should be levied according to the above regulations, and it is difficult to reduce or exempt. The funding difficulties mentioned in the original submission are not in accordance with the tax exemption regulations and the organization should seek other relief to comply with the regulations. As for the land without profits, our bureau, etc., have sent personnel to investigate. Once it is determined that the land has no profits and meets the requirements of Article 2, Section 2 of the Provisional Regulations on Land Price Tax Collection, we will jointly submit a request to your government for approval of tax exemption to maintain charitable activities. Is this appropriate? We will report to you the situation that it is difficult to reduce or exempt the land price tax on the organization's profitable land for your review.' This directive was issued by your government stating to proceed as proposed, and this batch of other reasons. We found that this case was previously discussed and decided by this Federation at a meeting, and has been repeatedly submitted to the Municipal Government and the Finance Bureau for review. In accordance with the above reasons, in addition to sending separate letters, we hereby inform you, and hope you will note accordingly."

Ministry of Communications Orders the Maritime Affairs Bureau to Stipulate Regulations for Ship Tax Inspection Certificates

Six Articles Promulgated for Compliance

Zhu Jiahua, Minister of Communications, regarding the Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau's proposal on whether to charge fees for the issuance, replacement, or modification of inspection documents and other certificates, requested instructions. It is now known that the Ministry has issued instructions to the Bureau yesterday. The original text is recorded as follows: "The submissions have been reviewed. The items listed in the report have been reviewed by the Ministry and instructions are given as follows: (1) When various certificates of ships under the Maritime Law are destroyed or lost, an application for reissue should be made according to the rules for loss, not replacement. (2) An application for replacement or reissue of a temporary inspection certificate for ships under the Maritime Law should be charged according to the rules for replacement or reissue of a ship inspection certificate. (3) There are no regulations for replacing ship inspection books. This is because once the inspection book is issued for the first time, there is no need to replace it. If there are any changes to the items recorded, they can be corrected in the original book without reissuing it. If the inspection book is damaged, it should be reissued according to the rules for loss and charged accordingly. (4) For ship passenger capacity certificates, except for changes in the passenger capacity, which require a new certificate, other changes to the recorded items should be corrected without charge. (5) When applying for correction of the items recorded in the temporary inspection book for small steamers, it should be handled according to Article 24 of the regulations on correcting inspection certificates and charged according to Article 43. (6) Correcting the ship name on various ship tonnage certificates and remeasurement forms, and correcting the inspection book for small steamers, are not regulated by the relevant regulations and should be exempt from charges. In addition to amending the attached fee schedule and issuing it for compliance, you are to take note. The table is kept on file. This order."

Taxpayers' Association Asks the Municipal Council to Cancel the One-Way Traffic Regulation on Hankou Road

Customers See It as a Hindrance, Greatly Affecting Shops

Do Not Merely Facilitate Staff's Access, Disregarding Citizens' Welfare

Since the implementation of one-way traffic on Hankou Road, the shops on the road have been greatly affected. They jointly wrote to the Taxpaying Chinese Association requesting the Municipal Council to cancel it. The Taxpayers' Association wrote to the Municipal Council requesting prompt cancellation. The original letter is recorded below:

Taxpayers' Association Letter: Regarding the one-way traffic on Hankou Road, we have received a letter from the shops on the road, jointly signed and stamped, requesting cancellation. After reviewing the points mentioned in the letter, they are indeed facts. The Municipal Council believes that "customers may feel inconvenienced at the beginning of the implementation of one-way traffic, but if given time and implemented for a long time, this inconvenience will gradually decrease." This statement has not been proven. It is no wonder that citizens are saying that the Municipal Council only knows how to facilitate the access of its staff, but has not considered the adverse effects on the business of the shops on the road. We are attaching the original letter from the shops on the road for your attention and prompt cancellation of the one-way traffic regulation on Hankou Road, so that the shops on the road will not continue to experience adverse effects on their business. Addressed to: Director-General of the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement

Shops' Letter: Since the implementation of one-way traffic on Hankou Road, traffic has been restricted, and customers see purchasing goods as a hindrance, leading to a decline in business for all shops on the road. Some have closed down, others have moved away, and vacant houses abound with no one interested. Those who have not yet closed down or moved are also in a precarious situation. We recall that when the one-way traffic was piloted in April 1930, the shops on the road jointly wrote to your association and the Chamber of Commerce for Transfer, requesting the Municipal Council to cancel it. We received a reply stating that customers may feel inconvenienced by the implementation of one-way traffic, but if given time and implemented for a long time, this inconvenience will gradually decrease. The request for cancellation was not granted. However, after investigation, most of the goods sold by the shops on this road are ordinary goods that are also available on nearby roads. Customers are willing to drive to purchase goods, but if they happen to encounter one-way traffic, they will abandon this road and go to another. Customers are the lifeblood of shops, and shops rely on customers to survive. The Municipal Council's implementation of one-way traffic on this road is indirectly putting the shops to death. The principle of municipal facilities is to seek the welfare of taxpayers. Now the Municipal Council has not sought the welfare of the shops and property owners who pay large amounts of property tax annually, but has already added to the destruction. For the sake of our own interests, we specially request your association to forward a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement, promptly cancelling the one-way traffic regulation on Hankou Road to maintain commerce. We are awaiting your urgent response. Addressed to: Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers Association
