Zhu Maocheng Clarifies the Truth About False Accusations

Zhu Maocheng of the Municipal Council's Rickshaw Affairs Committee, clarifies the truth about the false accusations, stating: "Last month, a rickshaw puller deflated tire incident occurred in this port. The Police Department of the Municipal Council filed a public prosecution against Zheng Fazhu and four others. The first instance trial concluded on the 30th of last month, and the verdict has been announced. However, because at the continued hearing of the case at the First Special District Court on the 24th of last month (i.e., Friday), I received reports afterward that two witnesses for the plaintiff, Xu Hanyuan and Wang Zhaosheng, etc., when giving testimony against the defendant Zheng Fazhu for fraud and embezzlement, one of them, Wang Zhaosheng, fabricated incidents out of thin air and greatly defamed me. The most important point was that when the defendant Zheng Fazhu paid the rickshaw license deposit on his behalf, he handed over 40 yuan to me in the name of a handling fee, etc. Because I was not present in court at the time, I did not have the opportunity to respond. After receiving the report, I specifically requested Judge Zhan, who was hearing the case, on the 30th of last month, whether I could issue a statement to clarify the truth to the public. Judge Zhan believed that the testimony was a minor issue and not related to the case, and that it was not necessary to issue a statement. Therefore, I still did not have the opportunity to respond. Later, the court announced the verdict. Except for the part about deflated tires, which had a separate verdict, all the points testified by Xu Hanyuan, Wang Zhaosheng, etc., were unfounded and were not punished. This shows that the court was also aware of the falsity of this defamation. I had no need to defend myself further. However, fearing that the outside world may not fully understand the truth, I am specially presenting the content of the statement that I wanted to issue to all sectors of society. According to the report, Wang Zhaosheng claimed that the rickshaw license deposit and the so-called handling fee were handed over to the defendant Zheng Fazhu at 8:00 AM on the 8th of last month, at the office of the Rickshaw Affairs Committee. The money was first handed over to Zheng Fazhu, who then handed it over to the committee. Later, they saw a person in a white suit escorting Zheng out, and later learned that the person in the white suit was me. However, according to the facts, the office of this committee does not open until the stipulated office hours of 8:30 AM. I also arrived at the office at 8:30 AM on that day as usual. Furthermore, the task of collecting license deposits is handled by the money collector sent by the Bureau's Tax Department. He collects the money every day and hands it over to the Tax Department. The procedure is very clear. Although some members of this committee sign the receipts, they never meet with the payers, and I have never inquired about how Wang Zhaosheng and Xu Hanyuan paid their deposits, nor have I signed their payment receipts. This is the factual process, which can be proved by all the staff of this committee. After receiving the report, I repeatedly wrote to the chairman of this committee, requesting a thorough investigation, and asked to convey it to the Director-General of the Bureau, requesting that he order an investigation to determine whether the testimony of the witnesses was true, and whether the Legal Department had obtained sufficient and reliable evidence before hastily ordering the witnesses to make such public defamatory statements in the dignified court. After this letter was sent, I received a reply from the chairman of this committee stating, 'The defamation against you is obviously without any basis, which does not require further comment from me and my colleague Wang Zhiren.' Also, 'The collection of deposits is handled by the money collector sent by the Tax Department. Although we are responsible for signing the receipts, the receipts of Xu Hanyuan and Wang Zhaosheng were not handled by you, nor were they signed by you. Therefore, the slander is even more absurd.' After the chairman of this committee received my second letter, in addition to requesting the Director-General of the Bureau to investigate the truth of the matter, he also expressed to the Director-General that he hoped that police lawyer Ru Baoyi would fully correct the situation and express his apologies at the next hearing of the case against Zheng Fazhu, etc. Later, he received a reply from the Director-General, stating, 'This is a completely unrelated matter to the Bureau's case, and the Bureau has no intention of suggesting that Zhu Maocheng would request or receive handling fees... As for making corrections at the next hearing, I have also discussed it in detail with the police lawyer, hoping that Ru Baoyi would follow the statement. However, according to the police lawyer, "If Ru Baoyi were to make such a statement at this time, it would show that the Municipal Council does not trust Wang Zhaosheng's testimony, and would lose the effect of this prosecution." The above includes the experience of the court, the investigation by the chairman of this committee, and the clarification by the Municipal Council. The truth is not difficult for discerning people to explore. However, what I want to say is that I have the responsibility to serve society and the sincere desire to improve society. If there is an opportunity, I will not refuse hard work and complaints. Slander and insinuations will never succeed in the light of day. A swarm of mosquitoes making noise is limited to dark corners. I believe that all members of society have sympathy."

Reasons for Reassessing Hotel Tax Amounts

The Municipal Council issued a statement regarding the dispute between the hotel industry association and the re-evaluated tax amounts. The facts are that the Municipal Council recently reviewed the municipal tax assessments for sixteen hotels. As a result of the review, the rent paid by five of them to the landlords was roughly consistent with the current market rent, and the tax amount was calculated according to the rent without any problems. The other three were self-built houses, and their current assessments were found to be quite fair, so they were not changed. The remaining eight had their assessments modified to be roughly the same as the assessments of the aforementioned five renters. One of the eight has already accepted the amount revised by the Bureau.

As for the other seven hotels that raised objections to the Municipal Council, all of them were self-built houses. The current revised assessments are based on the rents paid by similar houses in the vicinity. In other words, the tax amounts for these seven hotels are estimated using the same method as for all homeowner-occupied houses, that is, based on their rental value. In fact, the amount assessed this time is even lower than the equivalent actual rent paid.

The Hotel Industry Association proposed that the Municipal Council take a comprehensive consideration of the matter, but because the circumstances of each hotel are different, it is in fact necessary to review them separately. Anyone who disputes the tax amount has the right to appeal to the Tax Assessment Committee, which is an impartial body that can investigate all the facts and determine whether the assessed amount is fair.

The two hundred and seventh inspection was conducted at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on August 31, 1934, and the results are announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 77,841,337 silver dollars, including 71,151,2472 silver dollar notes and 6,633,8865 subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of reserve funds for convertible banknotes: 77,841,337 silver dollars, including 63,387,9337 silver dollars in cash reserves. The cash reserves are held in the Issuance Bureau of this bank (60,432,952 silver dollars), in branch banks in various ports (1,620,620 silver dollars), and in other banks (1,825,765 silver dollars). Collateral reserves: equivalent to 13,962,000 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold unit convertible banknotes issued: 373,324.70 customs gold units. Total amount of reserve funds for customs gold unit convertible banknotes: 373,324.70 customs gold units, including 7,351.95 taels of gold, equivalent to 373,324.70 customs gold units at a price of 50779. In accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve is 60% and the collateral reserve is 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60% and the collateral reserve is less than 40%, which is in accordance with the regulations. This report is hereby issued. September 1, 1934, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun; Supervisors, Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Hou, Xu."

Silk Industry Bank Creates Flexible Fixed Savings

A Type of "Half Deposit, Half Withdrawal" Savings

Excellent Interest Rates, Flexible and Convenient

Since its establishment, the Shanghai Silk Industry Bank, located at the corner of Hankou Road and Fujian Road, has been actively promoting thrift and savings. It has created various innovative programs, such as "Establishment Savings," "Education Savings," "Happiness Savings," and "Three Benefits Savings." These programs have been innovative in their approach and offered excellent interest rates, making them popular with depositors. As a result, the bank's savings business has exceeded expectations. In the last accounting period, deposits increased dramatically by one-fold, with fixed deposits accounting for nearly seven-tenths of the total. This demonstrates the deep trust that the public has in the bank. The bank has now created a new type of flexible fixed savings, also known as "half deposit, half withdrawal" savings. This type of savings is half fixed and half current. Therefore, if funds are needed, half of the deposit can be withdrawn at any time. An account can be opened with a deposit of ten silver dollars, and any amount can be deposited at any time thereafter. The interest rate is eight to one percent, with interest accruing on interest. This savings program incorporates the strengths of various existing programs, offering significant benefits to depositors. This fresh approach is unprecedented. The bank previously held a contest to solicit a "Song of Thrift" and new savings programs. This flexible fixed savings program was one of the winning entries. Other entries are still being reviewed.

New Pharmaceutical Association's Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce

The Shanghai New Pharmaceutical Industry Association sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "We have received your letter stating that the current Trademark Law is not applicable to the current industrial and commercial situation. You are soliciting opinions to be forwarded to the Trademark Law Research Committee for research. We have submitted the matter to a meeting and resolved that foreign companies have designated special terms for chemical drugs, but those terms that have been recognized worldwide as common names or have been included in the pharmacopoeias of various countries, such as the special terms 'Aspirin' and 'Vaseline,' should not be registered as exclusive trademarks by the Trademark Bureau. We are submitting this matter for your reference and transmission. Thank you for your attention."

Dehua Company Sells Suzhou Embroidery at Reduced Prices

Since the beginning of summer this year, there has been a severe drought and extreme heat, setting a record not seen in decades. The rural areas have been particularly affected. Suzhou embroidery is traditionally a rural sideline, with men farming and women embroidering to make a living. Now, there is no land to cultivate and no seeds to sow. Men and women in the villages are turning to sidelines. The Dehua Suzhou Embroidery Company, with branches in Suzhou and Shanghai, has been established for years. Manager Cao Yougao, mindful of the bankruptcy of the rural areas, cannot bear to stand idly by. He is promoting sales in the spirit of mutual assistance to provide relief. However, for several months, the goods have been piling up like mountains. He has had to transport all the new goods to Shanghai for sale at low prices, displaying them at the Dehua branch company in Huajin Lane, Third Avenue, for special low-priced sales. Patriotic citizens should visit early to acquire beautiful embroidery and help the rural areas. It is a win-win situation.

Entertainment

Nine Star Grand Theater Presents Min Opera: Min opera and Beijing opera share the same origin. During the Tang Dynasty, people from Fujian served in the inner court, performing in Beijing dialect. During the Ming Dynasty, it flowed into Fujian and formed its own genre. During the Qing Dynasty, it continued to be popular. After the establishment of the Republic of China, the troupes declined, and it gradually became a thing of the past. The Xin Guofeng Troupe is the most famous in Fujian, renowned in Guangdong and Guangxi. However, it has been absent in Shanghai. Mr. Lin, a Min businessman in Shanghai, has brought together the troupe from the south, summoning it to Shanghai. With the assistance of Shanghai gentlemen such as Zhang Xiaolin, the troupe will perform at the Nine Star Grand Theater to promote and entertain the people of Shanghai. The troupe has over a hundred male and female performers, all famous Min opera actors with a unique singing style, blending plain tones and Min music. The troupe has brought over a hundred boxes of brand-new costumes and two hundred sets of stage scenery, all made by the famous artist He Junfu, which are novel and unique. The Nine Star Grand Theater has recently been renovated with a new interior layout. All the performers have arrived and, after a short rest, will take the stage. In this cool weather, all the people of Shanghai are invited to witness it.

Reading Q&A

The Issue of Self-Study for Women After Marriage (Continued)

| Reply to Liu Xunyue |

Of course, such harsh criticisms are not without foundation; the facts before us inevitably lead to such conclusions. However, this is merely a superficial observation and cannot be considered the fundamental cause of women's decline. While women themselves should bear some responsibility for their unwillingness to enter society after leaving school, the main reason is that the shackles of the old society have not been completely removed from women, or perhaps not removed at all.

Everyone generally believes that society has already liberated women by allowing them to attend school and socialize with men. In reality, this is not the case. We should further ask: has society provided women with the same social status as men and granted them independent economic standing? If not, then the fundamental purpose of women's education in today's society is to produce decorations, or even modernized commodities. We often observe the distress many women experience after marriage, a distress that can even destroy their love for their husbands. This is because of the conflict between their thoughts and their environment. They have strong desires for knowledge or careers; they aspire to be complete individuals and hope to contribute to society. However, what avenues are open to them? What kind of work can they find? Needless to say, in this wave of unemployment and panic, even many male university graduates struggle to find their place, let alone women. In fact, society has never considered this for women. Under the constraints of this environment, knowledge is essentially useless to them, providing neither food nor clothing, and their pursuit of education becomes limited to finding a husband. Progressive women may still struggle in extreme distress, but conservative women can only submit by redirecting their educational aspirations towards serving their husbands and raising children, or even resorting to playing mahjong and watching movies. Like your cousin's wife, this may not be because she is content with her decline, but rather because of the disharmony in her life (the disharmony between her thoughts and her environment), she is intentionally seeking stimulation, which is very possible.

Of course, this fate of women is not necessarily determined only after marriage; it is decided as early as when their parents send them to school. Parents rarely send their daughters to school with the hope of them becoming a Ph.D. or a great scholar; mostly, it is for their daughter's happiness, hoping they can find a good husband. However, marriage, in a woman's entire life process, is the first step of contact with society, which also signifies the end of their school life. People always have hopes and dreams, and women in school are no exception, harboring a passion for learning. However, once they come into contact with society, they find that other hopes are dashed, and with no path ahead, their desire for knowledge naturally diminishes. Therefore, although marriage is not the cause of hindering women's pursuit of knowledge, it makes women unable to avoid stepping into their pre-arranged fate. | To be continued |

Children's Spring and Autumn Weekly

School Starts

— Wang Shouqiu

Children, time flies so fast, and in the blink of an eye, the summer vacation has already passed! In these fifty days, have you reviewed your lessons? Have you neglected your studies? You must reflect on this yourselves.

The summer vacation is over, and school is about to start again. Will you be able to advance to the next grade? Are you capable of handling the schoolwork with ease? You must also examine yourselves. If you have already been promoted, then you must continue to work hard in your studies. If you are unfortunately held back, then you must reverse your previous habits and start anew as a good student. The sage once said, "Do not hesitate to correct your mistakes." Who is a sage who can be without fault? However, one must know to correct one's mistakes. If one knowingly has faults but refuses to correct them, then that is bad!

Children, the fifty-day summer vacation is over, and now is the time for you to study hard! Children, work hard!

Introducing a Child to You

— Zhang Yide

Children! You probably all know Abraham Lincoln, the former President of the United States, right? But you may not know what he was like when he was a child. Let me tell you now!

He was born in Kentucky on February 12, 1809. He was very poor as a child, living in a small, dilapidated wooden house. A pile of messy straw served as his bed for the night. He was a very diligent worker, good at plowing, cutting grass, threshing, herding cattle, and other chores. There was nothing he couldn't do. He often helped his neighbors, so they liked him very much.

He was also very diligent in his studies, but he was too poor. He couldn't even afford to buy books, so he often borrowed them from others. If the person lived miles away, he would have to travel that far. Once, a book he borrowed, "The Biography of Washington," was accidentally damaged. He timidly begged the owner, who said to him, "If you work for me for three days, I'll give you the book." He got the book and diligently memorized it in his spare time, committing the entire book to memory.

He didn't have pens and paper to write with either. He used burnt charcoal to draw on the ground, walls, and stones. Although he was too poor to afford books, he studied diligently and perseveringly. Soon, he became the American President admired by all.

Children! Do you understand now? One must not give up on oneself, thinking that because there is no opportunity to study, one should not study. You should learn from Lincoln's hard work, and only then will you have a future! Children who have the opportunity to study, do not miss the time, and work hard!

— Chengming

Sit in a row, eat fruit, everyone, please eat Chinese fruit. Rights and interests can be protected, and loopholes can be prevented. Rather be hungry than eat those imported goods.

Children, high aspirations, respect teachers at school, respect elders at home. Brothers and sisters must be loving, and greet friends with a smile.

Not reading books is the most distressing, a blind person is laughed at. Unable to do great things, nor become a good old man. Do you think you will regret it?

Children, be diligent and thrifty. Study hard, all expenses must be frugal. Know that parents work hard to earn their sweat and blood money, providing tuition is already strained, how can you squander and waste money recklessly?

Small Animal Research

— Rongyu

(Can Earthworms Sing?) Min'er caught an earthworm and saw that its mouth was extremely small, not like it had a sound-producing organ. However, he saw the phrase "earthworm singing" clearly in ancient books, so he ran to ask his father.

Father said, "The sounds of insects are mostly produced by vibrating membranes beneath their wings. Earthworms have no membranes; there are no sound-producing organs in their mouths, so how can they sing? Originally, there is another kind of mole cricket in the soil, and its burrows are close to the earthworms. It has wings and membranes, and it vibrates its membranes to make music in its burrow. The ancients did not observe carefully and thought it was the earthworm singing. In reality, earthworms can only dig soil and absolutely cannot sing."

After listening to his father's words, Min'er realized that many things need to be investigated in person. "It is useless to believe everything in books."

(Distinguishing Beneficial and Harmful Birds) The small birds on the branches, with their beautiful feathers and melodious songs, are loved by everyone. However, among these many birds, some are beneficial to us, and some are harmful to us. How do we distinguish them?

Birds also need to eat and drink. Some like meat and specialize in pecking at small insects in the fields and trees. These birds indirectly help horticulture and farming, so they are beneficial. There are also birds that are vegetarians and specialize in pecking at good grains and fruits, etc. Aren't they directly harmful to humans?

Beneficial birds that peck at harmful insects mostly have pointed beaks and long tails, and they are very fast at killing. Swallows are representatives of beneficial birds. Harmful birds that peck at grains mostly have blunt beaks and short tails, and they are not very agile in flight. The sparrows we see every day are representatives of this type.

Cao Cao Leads Troops Down the Yangtze

— Xue Fan

Who doesn't say so, little brothers and sisters like to listen to stories, even more than eating and sleeping!

My sixth younger brother, like ordinary children, always pesters whoever comes, whether it's Sister-in-law Zhang or Sister Li, to tell him stories.

One day: Cousin Xu came to visit, and my sixth brother, as usual, stated his request:

"Brother! Do you have any new stories to tell me?"

"Yes! I'll tell you the story of Cao Cao going down the Yangtze."

"Good! Tell it!"

A sweet smile hung on the corner of his mouth, and my cousin also opened his mouth with a grinning smile:

"It is said that in the past, Cao Cao, 丨丨 do you know Cao Cao?" Cousin suddenly asked.

"I know, I know!" Sixth brother said quickly, "Isn't he a villain?"

"Yes! At that time, he was fighting with Zhou Yu, and Cao Cao led an army of 800,000 men down the Yangtze, in a mighty and imposing manner." Saying this, sixth brother smiled strangely.

"This army of 800,000 men suddenly had to cross a small wooden bridge. One by one, the 800,000 men crossed the bridge. The first one crossed, then the second one: The second one crossed, then the third one:: : Tak, tak,:: : Tak, tak,:: :"

Sixth brother became anxious and said, "What happened after the 800,000 men crossed the bridge?"

"How could 800,000 men cross it all at once? The third one crossed, then the fourth one: the fourth one crossed:: : Tak, tak,:: ; Tak, tak,:: :"

"Then it won't be finished even tomorrow!" Sixth brother said angrily.

"Of course, it's a small wooden bridge! How can it be fast?" Cousin smiled slyly.

"Okay, okay!" This time, sixth brother said boredly that he didn't want to listen, and quietly left.

Two Useless Things on the Human Body

— Ning Ziqiang

Children: The more things are used, the more effective they become. If they are not used, they are wasted, which is true for machines, and also true for the organs of the human body. For example, people have knowledge because of their brain organs, and animals do not have knowledge because they do not know how to use their brain organs. However, there are two things on our human body that are gradually being eliminated because we do not use them, such as the appendix and toes, are they purely useless things?

(1) Appendix: The appendix is the upper part of the large intestine, connecting to the small intestine above and connecting to the colon below. Because our ancestors were herbivores in the ancient times, they had to go through the appendix. Later, when they changed to eating meat, the appendix became a tumor-like thing, which is useless and has the risk of inflammation. If it is not removed, it can be fatal.

(2) Toes: Toes were also used by our ancestors to climb trees, but they have gradually been eliminated, resulting in shortening and degeneration into inch-long things, which will be completely eliminated in the future!

Clock Talk

— Xinyu

Children, at any time, you use the clock to do your work. But, were there clocks in primitive times? Where did the clock come from? Wouldn't you like to know?

In the beginning, there were no clocks in the world. People used the shadows of the sun and the positions of the stars to calculate the time. Later, they became smarter and used burning candles to measure the passage of time.

Babylon was the first to invent the clock, probably 2,800 years ago. However, the clocks at that time did not have hands. They relied on the sun to be used. It was a very simple sundial. At night, water flowing out of the pot was used to calculate the time, or milk, and some used sand.

Later, water clocks were invented, and the assembly was much more sophisticated than the flowing water pot. The clocks were engraved with degrees, but they were not very popular, and only nobles could use them.

After the Crusades, a clock with a hammer was brought from Palestine. This was a great progress in clocks, but no one knows who invented it. 650 years ago, there was a tower clock in the London Parliament. This was the first tower clock in the world.

250 years ago, there were portable clocks in the world. Then, watches appeared. A few years later, Galileo changed the hammer to a pendulum, so the clocks became more refined and accurate.

After that, there were clocks with minute hands up to 3.5 meters long, clocks with mechanical animals that could play the piano and tell the time, and clocks that could indicate the date and the position of the stars. Children, do you think it's strange? But, don't be surprised. The inventor of more strange and refined clocks in the world is you!

Children's Science Lecture

Light

— Linyin

When we see a fire burning, it emits a raging light. Where does this light come from? This is the expression of heat reaching its highest degree. When light shines into our eyes, it travels in a straight line. Therefore, when we watch movies in the cinema, as long as there is something blocking in front of us, we cannot see clearly. However, when light encounters an object, it can be reflected back and travel. This phenomenon is called the reflection of light. Suppose you and a friend are standing facing each other on the sand, with a distance of more than ten feet apart. Put a board in the middle and throw the ball on the board. The ball will definitely bounce back like (Figure 2). The friend standing opposite you will catch the ball. When he hits the ball on the board, you can catch the ball. Therefore, if you stand slightly off to the side, you cannot see your own image, but you can see the image of the person next to you. This is the reflection of light. As on the front of the mirror, you can see your own image, and the ball bounces straight up in the same direction as it was hit down (Figure 1).

The reflection of light can form a mirror. The ones we usually use are plane mirrors. If we use something that is not flat, then the reflection of light will be different. If you use a tin can and a copper spoon to look at your face, it will definitely be very funny. So some people use convex and concave mirrors to make funhouse mirrors (Figures 3 and 4).

If we place a pencil obliquely in a bowl of water, it looks like the pencil is bent upwards (Figure 5). In fact, the pencil has not changed in any way when placed in water. It is caused by the refraction of light. The reason is very simple. As shown in Figure 5, when light from A to C emerges from the water surface, it bends towards D to travel. Therefore, when looking along the straight line CD, it seems that A floats up to B. So the pencil inserted in the water seems to float up. If you put the pencil in a glass, it looks like the pencil is broken through the glass wall (Figure 6). This is because the light emitted from the pencil in the water is refracted when it goes from the water to the air. You can put a copper coin at the bottom of the bowl, put the bowl on the table, and slowly move back until you can't see the copper coin. Then ask someone to fill the bowl with water, and you can see the copper coin again. This is the best way to test the refraction of light.

The phenomenon changes again when light passes through a convex lens. If you try it in the way shown in (Figure 7). The candle flame is inverted after passing through the lens. This is a very interesting thing. The reason will be explained next time.

The Fly's Autobiography

— (Chen Yizhen)

I am a fly, wearing a shiny green coat, and my head is red, so my kind praise my beauty very much.

My nature is that I like dirty places the most. Trash cans, piles of dog manure, watermelon peels, and all unclean places are good places for me to breed seeds.

My body is covered with cholera germs, so the food I visit will leave a little bacteria, which will cause people to develop cholera when they eat it.

Because of these green reasons, people drive me away and hurt me when they see me, calling me the medium of cholera.

When I am eating and playing, I have to be on guard at all times against people's palms and rackets from coming to my body. Especially pay attention to children, because they like to catch me and feed me to ants.

I can hum tunes, and the tune is called "Buzzing Tune". If I find a pile of manure, I have to hum the tune happily and try this fresh food.

People are smart and have invented several machines to catch us, but no matter how smart you are, we still hum and fly around the garbage cans.

Correspondence from Rural Children

— Ziming

Early Autumn

Dear Children:

The sky is gradually getting higher, and cool golden winds are blowing from time to time; especially in the morning and evening, it feels very cool. The sultry heat will probably be eliminated in the shortest time.

Listen! The cicada's voice is hoarse, the green frog beats the final retreat drum, and the fireflies have also extinguished their light; so, is the earth lonely? No, definitely not! This is actually a very lively world: the weaver girl's "zhi zha zhi zha", the spinning girl's "sha sha sha", the cricket's "qu qu qu", hundreds of insects are chirping, as if holding an autumn music conference.

The cricket opened its jaws and fought to the death with its peers; with the spirit of fighting to the death, it decided the male and female, and the winner flapped its wings and sang loudly before returning. This kind of "fratricidal" action is certainly wrong, but since the other party has a fighting spirit, in order to protect one's own life, one can't care about anything, one can only fight hard! Then, when China is bullied by strong neighbors, it actually bows its hands and doesn't even fight a few rounds, doesn't it even have the courage of a cricket? Children! We should invigorate our vigor and vow not to be someone inferior to a cricket!" "Shoulder my gun and resist the enemy!"! The weather is hinting to us.

How to Keep the Brush Head from Falling Off

— Teng Jinbiao

Children: Are you very annoyed when you see the brush head falling off? Because it is not easy to put it back on after it falls off, but I have a method that can keep it from falling off forever. I will write it below now:

(1) Go to a traditional Chinese medicine store to buy some rosin, crush it, and then put some in the mouth of the brush handle where the brush head has fallen off.

(2) Smoke it over the fire to melt the rosin (be careful not to burn the brush handle).

(3) Rotate the brush handle so that the inside of the brush handle is covered with melted rosin.

(4) When the rosin is not yet solidified, immediately insert the brush head slowly, smoke it for a while, and it will be firm after a while.

After being installed like this, it will not fall off even if it is soaked in water or shaken vigorously. You children may wish to try it.

(1) A New Pencil

(2) Plan How to Use It

(3) Sharpened to Draw Pictures

(4) Shorter and Shorter When Sharpened

(5) Engraving on the Heart Will Always Be Broken

(6) This Is How Things Ended!

— Yi'an

China and Germany Exchange Graduate Students to Promote Cultural Exchange

The German Xiangbao Foundation, in order to promote cultural exchange between China and Germany, plans to send Ms. Kang to China to study Chinese literature and art. It has requested China to provide financial assistance and, at the same time, under the same conditions, also requested China to send a university student to Germany to study science for exchange. It is reported that the Chinese Ministry of Education has approved this exchange student research matter and will subsidize Miss Kang with 110 yuan per month from July of this year for a period of one year (research will be conducted at the Academia Sinica). It is also reported that the Chinese graduate student designated in Germany will also receive a monthly subsidy from Germany.

The Northeastern Students' Simple Cafeteria's Term Expires; Executive Yuan Orders the Ministry of Education to Take Over

After the September 18th Incident, many Northeastern students studying in Beiping and other places suffered hardships at home, and their economic sources were cut off. The Beiping Social Affairs Bureau, the Police Department, and other agencies investigated the situation of Northeastern students in various schools and reported to the Executive Yuan's Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee to try out the Northeastern Students' Simple Cafeteria to provide relief. The method was roughly as follows: Northeastern students first registered, went through the review procedures, and were issued registration certificates. Depending on the number of Northeastern students in each school, a simple cafeteria was set up in one school, or students from several schools were gathered at a suitable location to set up a simple cafeteria. Each student ate with a registration certificate. The trial period expired, and it was continued. After several years, the continuation period has expired again. Now, because the Ministry of Education had already established the Northeastern Youth Education Relief Office, which already has considerable relief measures for Northeastern students studying in Guannei, the Executive Yuan's Beiping Political Affairs Reorganization Committee reported the expiration of the Northeastern Students' Simple Cafeteria to the Executive Yuan, requesting that the Ministry of Education be ordered to include it in the relief case for Northeastern out-of-school impoverished youth and handle it together. After the Executive Yuan received the report, it yesterday ordered the Ministry of Education to take over the overall management.

Dai Chuanxian drafts an outline for Chinese scout education

The National Scout Association has been prepared, and the Ministry of Education has appointed Zhu Jiahua and fifteen others as directors. The association will be established soon, and the preparation office will be handed over soon. Dai Chuanxian, the director of the office, recognizing the importance of scout education, has drafted the "Outline for Chinese Scout Education" as an introduction to the office's work report. The following is an excerpt:

(1) The Chinese Scout aims to develop children's ability to act, cultivate good habits, make their personality noble, their knowledge rich, their physique healthy, and become young people with both wisdom, benevolence, and courage, to build a nation based on the Three Principles of the People, and to bring the world to universal harmony.

(2) The training principles of the Chinese Scout are as follows: (1) The Chinese Scout takes loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, and peace as the highest principles of training. (2) The Chinese Scout, whether individual or group, shall not participate in political activities with the qualifications or name of the scout, but it is not restricted if they participate as citizens in accordance with the law, and there is no interference with the religion of personal belief. (3) The Chinese Scout should adopt the educational proposition of children as the foundation and the methods of modern scientific education, based on the state of children's life, physiology, and psychology, as the criterion for implementing training, to cultivate the basic abilities needed to serve the nation-state and society. (4) Chinese Scout training learns by doing and does by learning, so children should be given as many opportunities as possible to come into actual contact with nature and society to cultivate their various life skills and proper attitudes towards people and things. (5) The Chinese Scout training aims to make children aware that serving others is the greatest happiness, and to take the three words "Be Prepared", "Do a Good Turn Daily", and "Service is the Purpose of Life" as their motto.

(3) The Chinese Scout oath is as follows: So-and-so vows to abide by the teachings of the Premier, strictly abide by the rules of the Chinese Scout, and practice the following three things throughout his life: First, practice the teachings of loyalty, filial piety, benevolence, love, trustworthiness, righteousness, and peace, and be a loyal citizen of the Republic of China. Second, help others and serve the public anytime, anywhere. Third, strive for the soundness of one's own knowledge, morality, and physique. Fourth, the Chinese Scout rules are as follows: (1) Honesty: The way to be a person lies in honesty. Whether doing things, speaking, or harboring intentions, one must be true and not deceive. (2) Loyalty and filial piety: One must be loyal to the country and filial to one's parents. (3) Helping others: Do one's best to help others, do at least one good deed every day, do not accept rewards, and do not take credit. (4) Benevolence and love: One must be affectionate to relatives and friends, kind to everyone, and care for things that are harmless to life. (5) Etiquette: One must be polite to people, and all responses should be in accordance with the rules. (6) Fairness: Understand things, distinguish right from wrong, treat people fairly, and handle things peacefully. (7) Obedience: One must strictly abide by group discipline and strictly obey national laws. (8) Happiness: One should always be happy, always smile, and remain calm no matter what difficulties one encounters. (9) Diligence and thrift: Be studious, practice diligently, endure hardships and be hardworking, do not waste time, and do not misuse money. (10) Courage: Do what is right without hesitation, do not be tempted by profit, do not be subdued by power, and do not care about success or failure. (11) Cleanliness: One's body, clothing, residence, and utensils must be clean, one's words must be cautious, and one's heart must be bright. (12) Public morality: Cherish public property, protect public interests, and do not hinder the public for personal convenience. The Premier said to the young people, "The first thing to do as a person is to set goals and do great things. One must take the country as one's own responsibility and shoulder the responsibility of building the future social cause." "What is called a great thing is to thoroughly accomplish whatever one studies, from beginning to end." The purpose of scout education is to create citizens who can shoulder great responsibilities for the country. Whether he is a farmer, a worker, a businessman, a soldier, an educator, or even a scholar or an official, he must be able to take on his own duties and careers and do well. Whether it is in standing in the world, to the family, to the society, to the country, one must always have good intentions, do good deeds, say good words, and be a good person. The four outlines listed above are good standards. Being able to do things at all times, consistently, and do them until old age and death is considered a good person. Things that are in line with these four outlines are considered good deeds. What one thinks in one's heart must not deviate from this, and that is considered a good intention. What one says in one's mouth must not deviate from this, and that is considered good words. If what one thinks in one's heart, what one says in one's mouth, and what one does are all integrated, constantly striving for self-improvement, and completing everything from beginning to end, then one has accomplished a great thing in life, is worthy of being a Chinese scout, and is worthy of being a citizen of the Republic of China.

Two children's libraries in Zhabei, Nanshi, opened yesterday

Chairman Pan Gongzhan reported the significance of the establishment

Representatives from the Education and Public Security Bureaus all gave speeches

The two children's libraries jointly organized by the Shanghai Children's Welfare Committee and the Children's Morning Post opened jointly at He'an Primary School at 9:00 am yesterday. The attendees included Director Pan of the Municipal Education Bureau, Hu Shuyi, Yin Guanzhi of the Public Security Bureau, Zhao Zengqi, curator of the First Library, Qian Fugong, curator of the Second Library, Xu Shushen, principal of He'an School, and more than 200 guests and students from various schools.

Chairman's report: After performing the ceremony as usual, Director Pan, the chairman, first reported, saying that the Children's Welfare Association and the Children's Morning Post, in view of the fact that small book stalls are everywhere in the city, and most of the books on the stalls are for children to borrow, this can prove that children who are literate always like to read, but the content of the small books on the stalls is not good, which has a bad influence on children after reading, which is very important. At the same time, there is no proper library in the society for children to read, so we jointly established two children's libraries, selected appropriate books, and provided children with reading and guidance on proper knowledge to supplement the shortcomings of school education. We also hope that those who come to the children's library to read are not only students in school, but also children who have no opportunity to go to school or have dropped out of school. We welcome them to the children's library. There are only two libraries now, and of course we will expand and popularize them at any time in the future, making them as common as primary schools. However, some primary schools already have libraries. These books are completely for the students in the school. We hope that the schools can break the boundaries of the school and also provide the books in the school for children outside the school. Then its effectiveness will of course be more common. This is not only a supplement to school education, but also an extension of school education outside the school. Secondly, we also want to run mobile book borrowing vehicles to transport books to various roads for children to read for free. In fact, each school can also do this method, and its power will be greater. With this kind of place to read books, the kind of bad small book stalls in the past can be gradually eliminated. Finally, we hope that in the future, there will be at least one or two dozen tutors in each children's library to guide children to read. In this way, the children's library is equivalent to a small school. If we want to get knowledge for children outside the school, we must promote this kind of fact, and so on.

Preparation process: Next, Qian Fugong, curator of the Second Library, reported on the preparation work, saying that the preparation time for the first and second children's libraries cost a total of three months. The start-up costs of the two libraries were allocated by the municipal government for 500 yuan, and the recurring expenses were given by the Children's Morning Post for 50 yuan per month. The major bookstores in the city actively donated books, and now a total of more than 5,000 books have been obtained. Now the first library is located in He'an Primary School, and the second library is located near Jinbo, Penglai Road, Nanshi.

Speeches from all walks of life: Then Yin Guanzhi, representative of the Public Security Bureau, gave a speech, and Hu Shuyi, representative of the Municipal Education Bureau, gave a speech, saying that foreign countries attach great importance to children's undertakings, and there is a children's bureau to manage all children's affairs. It is still difficult for our country to establish this kind of organization at present, and the Children's Welfare Association is established by various agencies, and its nature is similar to that of foreign children's bureaus, specializing in seeking happiness for children. Now the association and the Children's Morning Post jointly run a children's library to increase children's knowledge, which is very rare. I hope that all the children will develop the habit of reading and often go to the children's library to read, and so on. There are also Qian Shenzhi of the New China Bookstore and Xu Shushen of He'an Primary School who gave speeches, omitted.

Children's performance: At the end, Yu Xuan of He'an Primary School and Gu Senbao of Danhua Primary School gave speeches as children's representatives, and Zhao Zengqi, curator of the First Library, gave a reply. Then they performed recreational activities. The programs included He'an's national music ensemble, golden basket, harmonica, Shangwen's horseback riding to Shandong, blowing bubbles, Danhua's comedy, lively dance, Qingguang's anti-enemy rhythm, and dispersed at about 12 o'clock.

The first day of the Rotary Cup Shanghai International Tennis Tournament finals between China and the United States resulted in each country winning one singles match, leaving them evenly matched. Qiu Feihai Wins Big Against Squires

Qiu Feihai (China) Six to Two Six to One Six to Zero Squires (USA)

Qiu's control over Squires could be described as adept, directing the game as he wished. Qiu's steady baseline shots forced Squires to retreat to the baseline to cope. However, despite Squires's defeat, his improvement in skill is noteworthy. In the first set, Squires scored one game each at 2-1 and 3-2. Zheng Zhaojia Loses to Carlsen

Carlsen (USA) Four to Six Six to One Six to Two Six to Three Zheng Zhaojia (China)

Carlsen's skills are indeed above those of young Zheng. Whether it is serving, net play, half-volley, or lob shots, Carlsen is better and more confident than young Zheng. In addition, Carlsen's physical strength is also superior to Zheng. Young Zheng was consistently mediocre and lifeless yesterday. Except for the first set, he succumbed to Carlsen's racket in the second and third sets, unable to rally at all. Carlsen's lobs and volleys left young Zheng helpless. At crucial moments, he often sent the ball into the net himself. It is difficult to win by holding the baseline and waiting for the opponent to defeat himself. At the beginning of the fourth set, young Zheng tried to fight back, repeatedly trying to net play, but after 3-1, he fell into decline again. Carlsen won five consecutive games and won the match.

Municipal Party Asks City Government to Build Swimming Pool in Nanshi

The Municipal Party believes that promoting physical education is the top priority for strengthening the nation, and swimming is even more urgently needed. However, the city has a population of over three million, and there is still no municipal swimming pool. Now that the city government will build a large-scale sports ground in the city center, it is necessary to build a swimming pool in Nanshi, so that residents of Shanghai South can swim at any time. In addition, the Party Department of the First District submitted the same request, so it specifically sent a letter to the municipal government for investigation and handling. The original letter is recorded below: "To the Shanghai Municipal Government, according to the report from the Executive Committee of the First District of the Association, swimming is one of the physical exercises, which can not only forge a strong body and promote human health, but also improve self-cultivation, eliminate bad habits, and strengthen the race. Therefore, in recent years, the superiors have advocated encouragement and tried their best to guide, and the inferiors have risen up and gathered to participate, hoping to be strong citizens and wash away the shame of the sick man. It is found that the South District of this city has a vast area and a large population, and culture is developed. There is only one public sports venue, the Ximen Dajilu Public Sports Ground. The terrain of the field is insufficient, and the equipment is lacking, especially the failure to set up a swimming pool is regrettable. As a result, most swimmers have to go to other places, such as various concessions, which are under the jurisdiction of others, and the ticket fees are outflowed. If it is Gaohai Bridge Beach, it is too far away, the road is long and expensive. Those belonging to private individuals are mostly simple and dangerous. It is recently heard that the authorities intend to open a large-scale sports ground in the city center, including swimming, etc. The scope is wide, the project is complicated, and the date of establishment is far away, and the traffic is inconvenient. In order to facilitate the public in the South City, it is recommended that the authorities build a public swimming pool in the South City to meet the needs of the citizens. The Association has learned from this and submitted the matter to the superiors for transfer to the municipal government for approval at the 88th Standing Committee meeting. It is reasonable to record the case and submit it to your association for review and approval, and immediately transfer it to the municipal government for planning, so as to benefit the people and advocate sports. I beg you to follow it, which is for the public convenience. According to this, the corresponding letter is sent to you for investigation and handling. Sincerely yours, Shanghai Municipal Government."

Continuing to Fall 45 to 90 Cents

The supply of public debt fluctuates, depending on the sentiments of the people. The current situation is one of alarm, with short sellers being very active. Last Week's U.S. Cotton Market Quiet

A telegram from New York on August 31st reported on the cotton market for the week, stating: "The cotton market this week was relatively quiet. Any activity from either buyers or sellers would cause the market to react. At the beginning of the week, reports of high spot basis prices in the Southwest and scattered demand from fellow traders were factors maintaining the market condition. However, when the December contract reached 13.5 cents, selling increased, and the market price loosened. After the bulls closed out their positions, there was also some hedging selling in the South. The development of textile worker strikes, uncertainty about the next agricultural department report, and unsettling fluctuations in foreign exchange rates have limited the business of general merchants in the middle of the week. They are increasingly seeking to balance their transactions and wait for an opportunity. The strength of the basis prices in the Southwest is due to the fulfillment of contracts at the end of August and the beginning of September. Most of the new cotton shipments this week are destined for the Far East. The listing of new cotton is slightly delayed due to unfavorable weather. At the same time, merchants are unwilling to rush to sell due to strike news. Everyone believes that the limited demand from domestic cotton mills will lead to selling pressure, but government loans can protect it and prevent it from falling sharply."

Grains and Flour Plunge Sharply

After the opening of the flour market in the morning, prices for all months plummeted sharply. Although the quoted price for foreign wheat in Chicago was only about 3 cents, and Canadian wheat was better by 48 cents, the sentiment in the market and among those inside and outside the industry changed dramatically. The large amount of goods delivered in previous months had no inquiries for actual sales and were completely taken away by hedging accounts. The recent sluggishness of actual sales is due to the lack of purchasing power in rural areas, resulting in unusually sluggish intake. In addition, factory production has not decreased, leading to an increasing accumulation of goods. Therefore, after the opening price, the market saw a large decline. Major factories again took advantage of the situation and aggressively sold, causing near-term and far-term prices to fall sharply by 5 to 7 cents. When the market opened in the afternoon, the sentiment remained weak. Because of rain in various places in the inland areas, the inland merchants were also soft in their sentiment and sold off large quantities in various months. In addition, Amai's price was only 5.46 yuan, so the decline continued by another 2 to 3 cents in the middle of the session. However, towards the closing, the market slightly improved due to short covering. But given the current situation, due to the limited actual sales and the approaching foreign wheat prices, there is a general feeling that the previous sharp rise is unlikely to be repeated. As a result, this month fell by 8.25 cents compared to the end-of-month closing price, October fell by 9 cents, November fell by 9.25 cents, December fell by 9 cents, January fell by 8.5 cents, and February opened at 5.90 yuan and closed down by 4.75 cents.

After the opening of the wheat market in the morning, prices for all months fell sharply. Although the quoted price for foreign wheat in Chicago was only about 3 cents, and Canadian wheat was better by 48 cents, since the actual sales of flour have stopped, the consumption of wheat has also declined. The factories, after accumulating large amounts of flour and wheat, are taking a wait-and-see approach and do not want to compete. The market participants have long recognized that this situation is bound to fall, so when the opening price was set, this month was still as high as 8 jiao, but then the buyers sold off vigorously, and the price continued to decline. Later, affected by the loosening of flour prices, the price fell again. By the time of the closing, the price had fallen more than 1 jiao across the board. Looking back, the difference between the highest market value in August and the current value has reached 9 jiao, showing that an irrational rise must be subject to the same reaction. As a result, this month plummeted by 1 jiao and 8 fen, October fell by 1 jiao and 9 fen, November fell by 1 jiao and 8 fen, December fell by 1 jiao and 6 fen, and January fell by 1 jiao and 2 fen.

Foreign "Xian" Rice Continues to Fall 1-2 Jiao

|客幫内地完全停辦|

The market conditions for foreign "xian" rice yesterday saw a complete halt to inland operations by the "ke" merchant groups. The demand in this street was also weak. The hoarders only engaged in futures trading, and there was even a return of spot goods. The market softened immediately at the opening. The Yangtze River area also received rain, and the sources gradually increased. The autumn crops were excellent after the rain in the inland areas, which stabilized the sentiment. The early rice had been mostly harvested. For the time being, there was still rice stored from previous operations, so there was no need to transport and operate again. The market had a large amount of inventory, but little consumption, so the market price had to fall by 1-2 jiao. Fortunately, the hoarders were reluctant to sell after the small price drop, and this street bought on the dip, so the market was able to stabilize. In the overall market, 2,500 bags of various "ke xian" rice were opened, with 700 bags of spot foreign rice and 200 tons of futures. The stocks of small-grain and Annam japonica rice were small, and the market price was able to stabilize. The sources of "ke xian" rice gradually increased, and the price gradually decreased. In the futures market, many hoarders returned the stocks, with September Saigon at only 5.23 yuan and October at 5.3 yuan, a decrease of 1 jiao compared to the end of the previous month.

Main Reasons for Rising Asphalt Prices

Asphalt is suitable for autumn sales, and various places are purchasing from Hankou to meet the needs of the "tao" households. The inventory in Hankou is not large, and due to the hot weather, the goods from various production areas cannot be shipped, so the sources in Hankou cannot be gathered. The producers have not arrived in Hankou, so although the purchasers have needs, the sellers are few and far between. Recently, the price of Macheng oil has soared to 15.5 yuan, but this is not the actual market price. Because Taifeng is a guest goods, and the guest merchants have not arrived, the traders dare not specialize and deliberately raise the price to discourage the purchasers. It is likely that the formal market price will only be available after the autumn weather cools and the guest goods gather, and the guest merchants arrive. Heavy Jing is at 15.2-3 yuan per "ju," and Ping Jing is at 14.7-8 yuan. There are not many transactions either. The general situation is similar to Macheng. The Zhe asphalt is because the weather in the Jiaxing area is dry, and the harvest is greatly reduced. According to the tree heads, only 20-30% can be harvested in the future, so the Heben oil has soared to 22 yuan per "dan." Although the local traders are still purchasing from Hankou, the quantity is not large. Because the drought in Jiangsu and Zhejiang is so severe, the autumn and winter sales are bound to be greatly reduced, so they are unwilling to prepare too much. The selling price has gradually increased, with heavy Jing at 19 yuan per "ju," Ping Jing at 18.4 yuan, and Macheng oil at 17 yuan.

Peanut and Soybean Oil Weakening

The market conditions for peanut oil and soybean oil are in a state of increasing weakness. Yesterday, the market only opened for 450 pieces of peanut oil, including 50 pieces of Bo'er oil at a price of 11.6 yuan and 400 pieces of Juecang oil at a price of 11.4 yuan. The price was 6 jiao lower than the previous market. The stagnation of the oil market is due to the drought and cracking of inland river channels, making boat transportation impossible. There is no one asking about the outlets. It can only rely on the gradual sales on this street, so it is feared that the market atmosphere will not be easy to wake up for a while. At present, the bottom stock of soybean oil is increasing, estimated at more than 10,000 large and small pieces. The inventory of peanut oil is more than 1,000 pieces.

High Demand for Black and Purple Lamb's Wool, Prices Soar

Yesterday, the trading of woolen fabrics was brisk, both wholesale and retail. The standard market price remained the same as the previous day. The most popular item was black and purple lamb's wool. Because the inventory in the market was very short, the Sichuan merchant groups were actively searching for and operating on it, and the selling price soared. The yellow, black, and purple lamb's wool, which sold for about 6 yuan last year, has now soared to over 7 yuan, with the top-grade wool at 9.25 yuan. The popularity of the market can be said to be the best among the recent woolen fabrics. However, there is not much trading of the 9-yuan-plus top-grade goods on this street, because the buyers are mostly hesitant due to the high price, while the second-grade goods are in short supply and almost out of stock.

Competition in the Price of Hardware, English Galvanized Iron

Cheaper Than Japanese Goods

Recently, the local galvanized iron market has been dominated by Japanese goods. This is because their prices are cheaper than those of English and American goods. Consequently, customers and construction workers are happy to trade with them, and exchange dealers find them easier to sell, so they negotiate with them more often. As a result, English goods have become unusually quiet in the market. American goods, on the other hand, can still manage due to their superior quality, so their prices have not been greatly affected. However, British manufacturers, seeing the unfavorable environment and the impact of Japanese goods, have had to compete by lowering prices. Therefore, their cheaper goods are expected to arrive in mid-month, totaling more than 20,000 sheets, with a price of about $1.123 per seven-foot sheet and about $0.923 per six-foot sheet. Looking at the arrival price of Japanese goods, the lowest is $1.256 (seven feet) and $1.034 (six feet), which is more than a dime cheaper per sheet. Therefore, the smooth sales of English goods in the future can be predicted.
