Women's World

Cool Autumn, September

— Bi Yao

The unprecedented heat of more than sixty years made people "count the days until the west wind arrives" day after day. Now it's cool, and a rain brings the feeling of autumn.

This new autumn brings us some joy and some doubts.

Firstly: With the autumn coolness, women will no longer go barefoot and bare-legged, nor will they jump into bathing places with men. This way, public morals may be expected to change, saving officials in various places from worrying themselves sick.

Secondly: According to "Luxuriant Dew of the Spring and Autumn Annals," "Spring's atmosphere is loving, summer's atmosphere is joyful, autumn's atmosphere is stern, and winter's atmosphere is sorrowful." In these chaotic times, men of ambition are dispirited and mostly indulge in love and pleasure. It is useless to use sorrowful thoughts to reverse this declining trend; only the solemn atmosphere of autumn is the most suitable remedy.

However, on the other hand, early autumn is the time when new grains are harvested. Like this year, when Heaven has abandoned (?) our people, and floods and droughts occur together, how many farming families can pick up fallen rice ears? Who should first bear the brunt of this misfortune? Before the whole family, old and young, commits suicide by poisoning or hanging, they will inevitably sell their daughters, sell their daughters, sell their daughters. As a result, large cities, especially Shanghai, where Chinese and foreigners live together, will be filled with young prostitutes.

Furthermore, in the Northeast, since its fall on September 18, the suffering endured in the past three years and a thousand days can be described as profound. Now, the flag of the Blue Sky with a White Sun can no longer be seen. Imagining the women there, they are probably learning to sing the national anthem of the puppet state in a delicate voice, like Puyi's wife, while enduring shame and humiliation.

These internal and external sad situations call for every man and woman to step forward into society and train in various skills and abilities to save themselves and the country. Unexpectedly, just as a very few people were able to go out and support themselves, they encountered the prevailing idea that "women should return to the home"!

American aviator Miss White郎, because she couldn't find like-minded people here, quietly left China a few days ago. Our (women's) people, no matter where, are disappointing. Even if female thinkers, female educators, female revolutionaries, and female social workers from other countries come from afar, besides encountering pitiful or hateful prostitutes and modern types, what like-minded people can they find among our mothers and grandmothers?

Our people are destined to be submissive! All responsibilities of maintaining internal order, resisting external aggression, and issuing calls to charge are entrusted to a few superiors. What kind of national front formation is this?

Cool autumn, September, the cries of geese fill the fields, and in addition to hunger and thirst, there will be the oppression of cold. Cool autumn, September, the enemy's newly fattened warhorses will gallop into our fields. But our people are submitting to the current, submitting to the incompetent position of not hearing or asking about matters outside the home: unwilling to exhaust the functions of four hundred million people, lining up to save the four hundred million people's nation. This is how wasteful and ignorant it is here!

I Also Want to Talk About the "Good Wife, Wise Mother" System

— Li Hu

I cannot agree with the points that Ms. Yun Qi criticized in the previous "Good Wife, Wise Mother" system article. I hereby refute them:

The lady condemned this system as "a product of medieval feudal society, a tool used by men to restrict women to be instruments of their one-sided sexual desire, the most cunning means used by men to confine women into domestic slaves, and anyone who praises the good wife and wise mother system is reversing history."

On this point, the lady first committed the error of misinterpreting the four words "good wife, wise mother" and not recognizing the times. This "good wife, wise mother" system is indeed a product of medieval feudal society, and at that time, there were indeed such prejudiced and erroneous ideas. However, the lady does not know that history is advancing, and the emergence of any system is tied to relevant social background and timing; that is, it must adapt to the needs of the social environment in order to be promoted and supported by people. Therefore, its interpretation often changes with time and circumstance. The lady did not recognize that the current social environment does not require the adoption of this system, nor did she investigate what the true essence of the meaning of these four words "good wife, wise mother" is, and subjectively blindly misinterpreted them, leading to a deep and bitter hatred of this system. This is forgetting temporality and reversing history.

This "good wife, wise mother" system, according to modern interpretation, its true essence of meaning, I believe, is: a wise mother is one who teaches her children well, and a good wife is one who supports her husband's interests. She does bear the responsibility for all the trivial matters of the family, as well as the birth and education of children. However, it does not mean absolute obedience, hard work without complaint, and unwavering dedication until death. So, let's first examine whether the current social environment needs this "good wife, wise mother" system, which is also its true essence of meaning. Whether it is suitable for modernity.

Looking at the current social environment, most of the women who have been liberated and demand equal rights with men in all aspects are not large consumers of men's economic income, and most of them entrust their children to nannies and adopt a laissez-faire, uncaring attitude. Those who want to break the shackles of people and conform to the true essence of the meaning of "good wife, wise mother" are rare. May I ask if there is a more virulent consequence of liberation than this!

The "good wife, wise mother" system that is actually adopted, a wise mother, should take the obligation of teaching her children well as the goal, and urge them to make progress; a good wife should take the interests of the family as the premise, and cooperate, support, and strive together as the will. In the future, children and family will be the pillars and backbone of the country. A wise mother should take diligent teaching and patient guidance as her duty; a good wife should take assisting her husband and increasing the interests of the family as her principle. This is in line with the needs of a society like our country, which is poor, weak, and disorganized. It is not taking the three obediences and four virtues as the goal. If so, liberation and equality are complete, and rights and management are shared. Some achievements that have been achieved in long-term struggles (such as the right to freedom of marriage, the right to inheritance, the right to vote::) are not only not returned, but are also deeply rooted. So, what Ms. Yun Qi said: "Anyone who advocates restoring the good wife and wise mother system is actually advocating restoring the family system of the medieval feudal era and all the tools attached to it that oppress women." It is definitely an inaccurate, and even an empty statement.

As for the peasant families in our country's rural areas, under the cruel exploitation and oppression of capitalists, and under long-term and continuous unemployment, because the wife goes out to work as a lady or a nanny, the whole family has been torn apart, and there is no talk of any "good wife, wise mother" system. I believe that women in rural families in our country, from the perspective of cultural standards, cannot talk about enjoying equal rights with men in all aspects of economy, politics, and culture, but the true essence of the meaning of the modern "good wife, wise mother" system is completely in line with it.

Isn't men plowing and women weaving an expression of cooperating, supporting, and striving together with the interests of the family as the premise? Not hiring a nanny,

Under such exploitation and oppression, unwilling to sit idly by and watch her husband and children starve to death, she would rather abandon her husband and children, go out to work as an employee, and do her best to help. Can this not be said to be the ultimate expression of a good wife and wise mother, but a domestic slave? Only in this way can everyone do their best, both liberated and equal.

From the above points, does this good wife and wise mother system violate objective facts, should it be protested against, are we turning back the clock in history instead of moving forward, and is it a policy of fooling the people? I am afraid that Ms. Yun Qi's argument will be crushed by the wheels of history!

The Wives of the Soviet Union (Continued)

— Written by Auna Louise Strong, Translated by Liang Qiu

Soviet women are not respected because they are wives; even the wives of important people are not respected because of their husbands. When Stalin's wife died, the newspaper's black-edged obituary wrote her own name and career, only incidentally saying that she was Stalin's companion and comrade. Kalinin's wife gained her reputation for creating national farms and cultural centers in the Altai Mountains. In the Soviet Union, marriage is happy, but it is not a source of career.

The future and reputation of Soviet women are not obtained because they are wives, but because they are citizens. Family affairs, which are almost a legitimate profession in the United States, are only insignificant things that are not worthy of respect in our eyes. Household chores are shared by husband and wife. As for color, art, and music, we use them to decorate public places, such as cultural parks, rest areas, theaters, and factory clubs.

Our living situation often makes the wives of American engineers or workers who come to the Soviet Union tired. When the men are working happily in the factory, their wives feel lonely and bored. Their honorable profession - arranging a happy family for their husbands - is not needed in the Soviet Union. In the factories where men serve, they are seen as obstacles. Once, a leader of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs said to me: "These women (referring to the wives of American engineers or workers) often come to the office to pester us. Just because their husbands are useful people, they think they are great people. What's so great about it? Even Stalin's wife is not great! Parasites, parasites who only consume and do not produce, how much do they hinder the time of valuable workers!" These women either eventually found a job and enjoyed it, or pulled their husbands back to the United States.

Although we do not have the honor of being a wife or a housekeeper, we enjoy all the rights of honor in working as citizens, just like men. Throughout the Soviet Union, women hold positions everywhere: wives are village chiefs, collective farm leaders, chamber of commerce chairpersons, factory directors, judges in courts, doctors, or engineers. There is simply no gender distinction in work; schools and universities accept female students. Women work the same as men in any profession and receive the same wages as men. Nearly a hundred women have received the Order of the Red Star, which is awarded to people with advanced military achievements in the Soviet Union. Many women have received civil honors, the Order of Lenin, and the Order of the Red Star. Six thousand women are leaders of collective farms, one hundred thousand are elected as court officials, and four hundred thousand are officials in local Soviets. Female students account for seventy-one and a quarter of the total number of students in medical schools, and it is expected that most of the future doctors will be women. Women have gone to the Arctic to explore. Alan Rozanova was the first female Arctic explorer. She spent a year in the icy and snowy world, sailing on the Abrikov icebreaker on two routes in Northeast and Northwest Asia. Some people encountered many Soviet female geographers at the top of the world. A woman gave birth to a son on the Chelyuskin icebreaker.

The women's independence movement, which is developing very slowly in various countries around the world, has developed rapidly in the Soviet Union due to the rapid development of industry.

丨Farmlands were combined into mechanized and industrialized collective farms in five years, where women worked the same as men and received compensation. Under the Soviet political system, the peasant women who finally felt that they had equal rights gradually realized the meaning of having an independent income.

Because of the creation of collective farms, thirty million peasant women from Leningrad to Vladivostok felt that they could live safely without a husband. The men's last fortress - an old-fashioned family, a male-centered, patriarchal family - has reached its end for the sake of women's equality and independence. This is probably what moralists in countries outside the Soviet Union are most heartbroken about.

Parents' University and Wise Mother, Good Wife

— Fei

Good and wise are both very good words, but it is suspicious to only say "wise mother, good wife" and not "good husband, wise father." It is even more suspicious to label it as an ideology and promote it. Is this what is called: "Confirming the principle of gender equality and promoting the development of women's rights"? I don't understand it. Ever since the slogan "Women return to the family" was put forward, the role and meaning of "Wise Mother, Good Wife Ideology" became clear. Okay, if you want to return to the family, then return to the family. But what are you going back to do? Farmers are bankrupt, and many workers have no home, so let's not talk about them. Speaking of those who have a home: "Ahem! Bring me a cup of tea!" "Bring me a cigarette丨light it!" Seems very arrogant, aren't you ashamed? Making beds, folding quilts, sweeping the courtyard, women can certainly do it, but men can also do it. Speaking of clothes: Western suits are certainly not something a good wife is familiar with, and Chinese-style clothes are still made by a tailor. Socks, cloth-made ones, have long been worn by no one. As for shoes, whether cloth or leather, they are all well-fitting products from shoe stores. And scarves, needless to say, there is no need to bother the wife丨good wife to worry about. Even small things like handkerchiefs, with new styles and many colors, are readily available on the market丨and they are cheap and of good quality. Speaking of eating: Rice, noodles, and food, as well as tea and snacks, anything slightly tasty has long been bought from the neighborhood. As for dishes, everything, no matter how wise the wife is, she can't compare to the chef. In an industrial society, restaurants, eateries, and lunch providers have simply replaced the family kitchen. The so-called "internal affairs" seems to be intentionally made empty by Father Time. Speaking of children's love: This is originally a universal human feeling, and it should be treated equally. If they also say: You should also stay at home with me all day long! Let's not do anything else! How would that work? It is impossible to be a good wife. Then, let's talk about wise mothers: Once a wife gives birth to a child, she gets the title of mother, and thus the husband becomes a father. Of course, the husband cannot raise children, but the husband's relationship to raising children is also very important. For example, if he doesn't know about physiology, hygiene, and hygiene, it will bring misfortune or disaster to the mother and child. After the child is born, they need to be raised and educated, which requires a wise mother. In fact, the guys who become fathers, besides not having milk, can not only do the tasks of a wise mother, but can also do them very well. Let's take the heavy task as an example: The most difficult thing in raising a child is dealing with children's illnesses. Taking Shanghai as an example, the best pediatricians are men, not women. Secondly, there is education. Not to mention the distant past, the German Troebel, who first created kindergartens, was not a woman. Even in terms of Chinese experts in child education, isn't Mr. Chen Heqin the first to be recommended? As for washing diapers, changing poop bags, and even hugging and teasing, it is not divided by gender, everyone can do it, it's just a matter of whether or not they do it. From this, it can be seen that a mother can be wise, not only can women do it, but men can especially do it. I think: Ten months of pregnancy, and then going through life and death during childbirth, women's maternal tasks can be considered the most difficult and greatest. After the child is born, let the man raise it, wouldn't that be very fair?

From the facts mentioned above, we know that: The so-called "housework" has been transformed into social industry due to human evolution and social progress. The responsibilities of women in the past have mostly become specialized knowledge. What was previously considered things that women should do, men can now do丨Things that were previously required of women (such as raising infants), men are now happy to do and do them very well. This is what the facts tell us: The era of good wives and wise mothers is over! There is nothing for women to do when they return to the family! For the sake of human happiness 丨especially for the children, we should have an education that is more suitable for modern times! This, in addition to universally implementing "human" education regardless of gender, we should run a "Parents' School!"

"Parents' University" was recently established in Soviet Russia (various newspapers published this news at the end of June, and Chen Xi of the Xinwen Chenbao also wrote an article about it), which has already attracted the attention of the Chinese people. Soviet Russia is a country that encourages women to go to society. It is said that more than one-third of the female students in their universities are female scientists with national credentials, totaling 7,000. More than 90 people are leaders of national scientific institutions! There are 20,000 registered cases of women making technical inventions! There are more women in health and education institutions. Women's participation in other agricultural, industrial, political, and police circles has long been known to us. This proves that it is completely a prejudice丨not in line with the facts that women are only suitable for managing the family and raising children. They丨Soviet Russia pay attention to children's happiness no less than other countries, at least not weaker than us. For the sake of public child care, they have universally established "nurseries." Then, creating a "Parents' University," as the name suggests, is undoubtedly thinking about their small citizens.

Using school education and scientific knowledge to teach people all the intelligence of being parents, so that every educated person can acquire specialized knowledge, whether in the family or in society. How can this be compared with the one-sided and unsuitable "Wise Mother, Good Wife Education" of the times? Therefore, I think that instead of blindly shouting about "Wise Mother, Good Wife" education, it is better to advocate running a "Parents' University."

A Visit to Shanghai's First Nursery

— Wu

The children are unusually healthy

Family members can rest easy

Shanghai Children's Welfare Association's First Nursery has been open for several months, but I haven't had the chance to visit it due to being burdened by life. Recently, I took the opportunity to attend the Confucius Memorial Meeting and drove there. Walking into the reception room, Director Yang of the nursery greeted me with a beaming smile, waving a large palm-leaf fan. She looked at least fifty years old, but her energy was vaguely the same as a young person's.

After sitting down, we exchanged pleasantries as usual. Then, I hurriedly asked everything I wanted to know as much as possible.

According to Director Yang's sincere answer: "The organization of the nursery is very simple. The director is a volunteer. In addition, there is one clerk, one nanny director, one teaching assistant, six nurses, and four wet nurses: The nanny director and the teaching assistant are in charge of teaching, and the nurses are all from medical schools and are in charge of childcare.

"The total number of children in the nursery is sixty (half of whom are infants). They are divided into three groups for education and care. From birth to one year old is considered infants, one to three years old is toddlers, and three to six years old is kindergarten students (only one is six years old). The children's families are mostly from the academic community, followed by business, government, and military.

"In terms of economy, the monthly expenditure is 1,000 yuan, and the tuition income is only 400 yuan. Therefore, even though each child costs eight yuan, the nursery actually subsidizes a lot. First of all, the milk powder alone costs about 12 yuan per child on average.

"In terms of equipment, we have everything ordinary. The only shortcoming is that we don't have a garden."

At this point, I felt that the conversation was coming to an end, so I stood up and asked to visit the various rooms.

"Welcome!" Director Yang stood up before I finished speaking.

First, we visited the washroom, dining room, and classroom, which were all decorated very simply. Then, we stepped onto the stairs.

"Director Yang, recently there have been some rumors outside that the children have become thinner after coming here. Is that true?" I suddenly remembered a friend's casual remark and asked as we walked.

"Hmm!" Director Yang seemed a little surprised, but then she calmed down and said: "This can be said to be half rumor and half misunderstanding. For example, if you have a child and you change to a new wet nurse, wouldn't the child become thinner due to physical and milk reasons? So, even if there are sometimes one or two thinner children in our nursery, it is at most for this reason. Of course, I'm not saying that we're doing things perfectly, but in reality::? Oh, I can tell you that there is not a single thin child right now. Fortunately, the facts will prove it to you right away, you see."

At this moment, the children's bedroom was in front of us. Because it was nap time, all the children were sleeping peacefully.

The light in the room was very soft, and the small iron beds were neatly arranged. When our legs stepped into the door, the children who were awake all looked up with happy faces, their eyes spinning around as they looked at us, their tender white hands reaching for the railings on both sides of the bed. Lively and healthy, it was impossible not to smile with satisfaction from the bottom of my heart. Who can say that these children are weak?

Walking to the nursery, it was even more endearing. Every little angel was fast asleep. In a cradle near the door, it is said that the one sleeping is the little cat just born to Ms. Ye Mao Wang Renmei.

Before leaving, in order to get a more concrete answer to the question of whether China urgently needs nurseries, I asked about the reasons for keeping the children. Director Yang showed me a recent statistical table, which I am copying below for scholars to study.

Due to job constraints 18

Want to receive good education 12

Because of household chores 6

Do not trust wet nurses 7

Too many children 5

No one to take care of mother 4

Mother sick 3

Unable to balance studies 2

Save money 1

However, this is not a labor nursery. The infants and toddlers of truly poor laborers are still unable to enter. Finally, Director Yang said that the nursery "has been full soon after its establishment." This proves the urgent need for nurseries in today's society.

Random Chats While Enjoying the Cool Air

— First

On hot summer evenings, after dinner, I often take a banana leaf fan and sit in the alley to enjoy the cool air. Here, there are no ladies or misses; a row of nannies and young maids are sitting. Running and jumping around are those lively children.

The nannies chat with each other, and the young maids joke together. They see each other every day and often rest in the alley, becoming thoroughly acquainted. Only I am lonely. I sit silently, mechanically waving my fan, but the heat does not diminish at all; and the vexation in my heart makes the heat even more unbearable. I am a little envious of that joyful group; they talk and laugh, forgetting the fatigue and the onslaught of the heat. Why can't I join their group and talk and laugh with them? So I walked closer to the young maids, teasing the baby and talking to the young maid. But I immediately felt uncomfortable: they treated me as they would treat their master, with fear and trepidation in their hearts; and I couldn't help but feel a little uneasy myself.

We cannot get close to lower-class women, nor can we understand their suffering, if we cannot abandon those feudal ideas of being first-class and so on.

In order to understand the lives of these nannies and young maids, I often look for opportunities to talk to them. Now, several of them often come to me to write letters home for them. I have become very familiar with them. Their lives are really as they themselves say: "Three times more bitter than Coptis chinensis." But their efforts, their struggles, and their spirit of struggling in a difficult life really make us admire them! Therefore, I want to introduce the conversations of a few to everyone; if there are people who sympathize with them and cry out their suffering and injustice in unison, improve their treatment a little, and elevate their personality a little, that is my original intention in writing this article.

丨Peng Ma丨

Peng Ma is the nanny in my landlord's house. She has been helping in the employer's house for more than a year. Her niece is also working here as a young maid, taking care of the children for the landlady.

She, about forty years old, is from Hunan, speaking with a strong local accent. A pair of small feet like swollen rotten eggplants, as if she had never washed her feet or changed her socks, her socks covered in dust. She spends almost all day in the kitchen; the weather is so hot that she must bake by the stove. She gets up before dawn to wash clothes. When I get up at six o'clock, she has already cooked porridge and gone to the market to buy vegetables. At night, she goes to bed later than anyone else: she has to wait for the madam to return at midnight or one o'clock before she can feel at ease to sleep.

One day, she came down from the drying rack after drying clothes, passing by my door; I asked her when she wanted me to write a letter? She knew I had spare time to write a letter for her, so she walked into my room and sat down. As soon as she sat down, she took a deep breath. It was as if she had been so busy all day that she couldn't breathe, and now that she was sitting down to rest, she finally exhaled.

"Is Madam not at home?"

"Mrs. Zhang went to play mahjong."

"Your son's writing has improved a lot." (To be continued)
